
1a1(mdo 'grel): maung+gal gyis bus mdzad pa'i gdags pa'i bstan bcos bzhugs so//
1b1(mdo 'grel): rgya gar skad du/ lo ka pradz+nyA ba ti/ bod skad du/ 'jig rten bzhag pa/ bam po dang po/ bcom
1b2(mdo 'grel): ldan 'das shAkya thub pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /de nas stong rnams dang ni rol mtsho dang/ /ngan song gsum dang gling dang
1b3(mdo 'grel): shing/ /dge 'tshal dang ni mkha' lding dang/ /rgyal chen grong dang 'dun sa rnams/ /'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus
1b4(mdo 'grel): gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na/ rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra
2a1(mdo 'grel): ba na bzhugs te/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis dge slong rnams la bka' stsal ba/ dge
2a2(mdo 'grel): slong dag 'jig rten gyi khams ni gsum po 'di dag yin te/ gang dag yin zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ stong chung ngu'i 'jig
2a3(mdo 'grel): rten gyi khams dang/ stong gnyis pa bar ma'i 'jig rten gyi khams dang/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten
2a4(mdo 'grel): gyi khams so/ /stong chung ngu'i 'jig rten gyi khams gang zhe na/ stong gsum gyi 'jig rten gyi khams na nyi ma rnam par snang ba
2b1(mdo 'grel): rnams kun tu 'khor zhing phyogs snang bar byed pa yod pa de nyid kyi yin te/ zla ba stong dang/ nyi ma stong dang/ ri'i rgyal po ri rab stong dang/ shar gyi lus
2b2(mdo 'grel): 'phags pa stong dang/ lho'i 'dzam bu'i gling stong dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod stong dang/ byang gi sgra mi snyan stong dang/ rgyal chen bzhi pa'i lha ris stong dang/
2b3(mdo 'grel): sum cu rtsa gsum pa stong dang/ 'thab bral ba stong dang/ dga' ldan pa stong dang/ 'phrul dga' ba stong dang/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa stong dang/ tshangs
2b4(mdo 'grel): pa'i 'jig rten stong ste/ dge slong dag 'di ni stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams zhes bya'o/ /stong gnyis pa bar ma'i 'jig rten gyi khams gang zhe na/ stong
2b5(mdo 'grel): chung ngu'i 'jig rten gyi khams stong gang yin pa don stong gnyis pa bar ma'i 'jig rten gyi khams zhes bya'o/ /stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i khams gang
3a1(mdo 'grel): zhe na/ dge slong dag stong gnyis pa bar ma'i 'jig rten gyi khams stong gang yin pa de ni stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams zhes
3a2(mdo 'grel): bya'o/ /dge slong dag de lta bu'i stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams rnams shar phyogs su mdza' med cing mu med la/ 'jig pa'am/ zhig par
3a3(mdo 'grel): gnas shing/ chags pa 'am 'chags rab gnas te/ gzhan 'jig cing gzhan zhig par gnas/ gzhan chags shing gzhan 'chags par gnas so/ /dge slong
3a4(mdo 'grel): dag 'di lta bur stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams lho dang/ nub dang/ byang gi phyogs su mdza' med cing mu med la/ 'jig pa 'am/ zhig par gnas
3a5(mdo 'grel): shing/ chags pa'am 'chags par gnas te/ gzhan 'jig cing gzhan zhig par gnas la/ gzhan chags shing gzhan 'chags par gnas so/ /dge slong dag
3b1(mdo 'grel): nam mkha' las char pa'i 'bru'i shing rta'i srog shing tsam 'bab ste/ chu'i rgyun rnams rab tu 'bab pa na bar chad med pa de bzhin du/ dge slong dag ngas lha'i mig rnam par dag pa mi las 'das pas
3b2(mdo 'grel): shar phyogs su de lta bu stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams mdza' med cing mu med pa/ gzhan 'jig pa 'am zhig par gnas shing/ chags pa'am/ 'chags par gnas la/ gzhan
3b3(mdo 'grel): 'jig cing gzhan zhig par gnas la/ gzhan 'chags shing gzhan chags par gnas pa dang/ de bzhin du lho dang/ nub dang/ byang phyogs su de snyed kyi stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi
3b4(mdo 'grel): khams rnams mdza' med cing mu med la/ 'jig pa'am/ zhig par gnas shing/ chags pa'am 'chags par gnas te/ gzhan 'jig cing gzhan zhig par gnas la/ gzhan 'chags shing
3b5(mdo 'grel): gzhan chags par gnas pa dag kyang mthong ngo zhes bka' stsal nas/ bcom ldan 'das nang du yang dag 'jog pa'i phyir gnas khang nang du gshegs/ /de'i tshe na/ tshe dang ldan pa maung+gal ya na chen po 'khor
3b6(mdo 'grel): de nyid kyi nang du 'dus par gyur te 'dug go /de nas tshe dang ldan pa maung+gal yan chen pos dge slong rnams la smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa dag ji tsam du bcom ldan 'das kyis legs par bstan pa dang/ 'di
4a1(mdo 'grel): ltar shing rta'i srog shing gi dpes bstan pa la ni legs te ngo mtshar to/ /de la stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na ri chen po nyis stong yod de/ ri'i rgyal po ri rab stong dang/ khor yug gi
4a2(mdo 'grel): ri stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na/ rgya mtsho chen po nyis stong yod de/ nang gi rgya mtsho chen po stong dang/ phyi rol gyi rgya mtsho chen po stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na ngan song
4a3(mdo 'grel): gsum stong yod de/ sems can dmyal ba stong dang/ dud 'gro stong dang/ yi dwags stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na gling chen po bzhi stong yod de/ shar gyi lus 'phags po stong dang/ lho'i 'dzam+bu'i
4a4(mdo 'grel): gling stong dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod stong dang/ byang gi sgra mi snyan stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na shing chen po bzhi stong yod de/ 'dzam+bu'i gling ba'i shing rgya mtsho'i 'gram gyi shal ma li chen po stong
4a5(mdo 'grel): dang/ lha ma yin gyi ris kyi tsita pa ta li stong dang/ sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i sa rtol stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na klu'i rigs bzhi stong yod de/ klu'i rig sgo nga las skye ba stong dang/ mngal nas skye ba stong dang/ drod gsher las
4a6(mdo 'grel): skye ba stong dang/ rdzus te skye ba stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na nam mkha' lding gi rigs bzhi stong yod de/ nam mkha' i lding gi rigs sgo nga las skye ba stong dang/ mnga' nas skye ba stong dang/ drod gsher las skye ba stong dang/ rdzus ste skye
4b1(mdo 'grel): bstod rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na rgyal po chen po bzhi stong yod de/ yul 'khor srung stong dang/ 'phags skyes po stong dang/ mig mi bzang stong dang/ rnam thos kyi bu stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams
4b2(mdo 'grel): na 'gro ba lnga stong yod de/ sems can dmyal ba'i 'gro ba stong dang/ dud 'gro dang/ yi dags dang/ lha dang/ mi'i 'gro ba stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na 'dun sa chen po nyis stong yod de/ lha'i 'dun sa chos bzangs stong dang/ lha
4b3(mdo 'grel): ma yin gyi 'dun sa nor bzangs zhes bya ba stong rnams so/ /'jig rten bzhag pa las tshigs dang po'o/ /mdo la/ skye gnas ri dang rol mtsho dang/ /de bzhin sems can dmyal brgyad gzhan/ /sems can gnas dgu rab bshad de/ /las lam
4b4(mdo 'grel): bcu po de bzhin no/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na 'dod pa'i skyes gnas gsum yod de/ gsum gang zhe na/ sems can 'dod pa nye bar gnas pa dag yod de/ gang dag 'dod pa nye bar gnas pa rnams la dbang phyug gis dbang byed
4b5(mdo 'grel): pa ste/ 'di lta ste/ mi kha cig dang/ lha rnams so/ /'di ni 'dod pa'i skye gnas dang po'o/ /sems 'dod pas sprul ba dag yod de/ gang dag 'dod pas sprul pa rnams la dbang phyug gis dbang byed pa dag ste/ 'di lta ste/ 'phrul dga' i lha rnams so//
4b6(mdo 'grel): 'di ni 'dod pa'i skye gnas gnyis pa'o/ /sems can 'dod pa'i sprul ba gzhan dag yod de/ gang dag 'dod pa gzhan gyis sprul pa rnams la dbang phyug gis dbang byed pa dag ste/ 'di lta ste/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams so/ /'di
4b7(mdo 'grel): ni 'dod pa'i skye gnas gsum pa'o/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na bde ba'i skye gnas gsum yod de/ sems can gang dag lus 'di nyid la dben pa las skyes pa'i dga' ba dang/ bde ba las brlan par byed cing yongs su brlan par byed
5a1(mdo 'grel): de/ yongs su tshim par byed cing yongs su khyab par byed pa dag yod do/ /de dag lus 'di nyid la dpen pa las skyes pa'i dga' ba dang/ bde bas brlan par byas shing yongs su brlan par byas te/ yongs su tshim par
5a2(mdo 'grel): byas shing yongs su khyab par byas nas bde bar reg pa la gnas so/ /de dag bde ba de dang/ bde ba la gnas pa des tshe ring zhing yun ring por gnas te/ 'di lta ste/ tshangs ris kyi lha rnams so/ /'di ni bde ba'i skye gnas dang po'o/ /sems
5a3(mdo 'grel): can gang dag lus 'di nyid la ting nge 'dzin las skyes pa'i dga' ba dang/ bde bas brlan par byed cing yongs su brlan par byed de yongs su tshim par byed cing yongs su khyab par byed pa dag yod do/ /de dag lus 'di nyid la ting nge
5a4(mdo 'grel): 'dzin las skyes pa'i dga' ba dang/ bde bas brlan par byas shing yongs su brlan par byas te/ yongs su tshim par byas shing yongs su khyab par byas nas bde bar reg pa la gnas so/ /de dag bde ba dang bde ba la gnas pa des tshe
5a5(mdo 'grel): ring zhing yun ring por gnas te/ 'di lta ste/ 'od gsal gyi lha rnams so/ /'di ni bde ba'i skye gnas gnyis pa'o/ /sems can gang dag lus 'di nyid la dga' ba med pa'i bde bas brlan par byed pa dang/ yongs su brlan par byed de/ yongs
5a6(mdo 'grel): su tshim par byed cing yongs su khyab par byed pa dag yod do/ /de dag lus 'di nyid la dga' ba med pa'i bde bar brlan par byas shing yongs su brlan par byas te/ yongs su tshim par byas shing yongs su khyab par byas nas bde bar reg
5a7(mdo 'grel): pa la gnas so/ /de dag bde ba de dang bde ba la gnas pa de'i tshe ring zhing yun ring du gnas te/ 'di lta ste/ dge rgyas kyi lha rnams so/ /'di ni bde ba'i skye gnas gsum pa'o/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na gser gyi ri chen po
5b1(mdo 'grel): bdun stong yod de/ ri'i rgyal po gnya' shing 'dzin stong dang/ gshol mda''dzin stong dang/ seng ldeng can stong dang/ blta na sdug stong dang/ rta rna ri stong dang/ mu khyud 'dzin stong dang/ ri'i rgyal po rnam par 'dud stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phung kyi 'jig
5b2(mdo 'grel): rten gyi khams na rol mtsho chen po bdun stong yod de/ gnya' shing 'dzin gyi rol mtsho stong dang/ gshol mda''dzin gyi stong dang/ seng ldeng can gyi stong dang/ blta na sdug gi stong dang/ rta rna ri'i stong dang/ mu khyud 'dzin gyi stong dang/ rnam par 'dud kyi
5b3(mdo 'grel): rol mtsho stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na sems can dmyal ba chen po rgyad stong yod de/ sems can dmyal ba chen po yang sos stong dang/ thig nag stong dang/ bsdus gzhom stong dang/ ngu 'bod stong dang/ ngu 'bod chen po stong
5b4(mdo 'grel): dang/ tsha ba stong dang/ rab tu tsha ba stong dang/ sems can dmyal ba mnar med pa stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phung kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na sems can gyi gnas dgu stong yod de/ sems can gzugs yod pa lus tha dad cing 'du shes tha dad pa dag yod
5b5(mdo 'grel): de/ 'di lta ste/ mi rnams dang/ lha kha cig go /'di ni sems can gyi gnas dang po'o/ /sems can gzugs yod pa lus tha dad la 'du shes gcig pa dag yod de/ 'di lta ste/ tshangs ris kyi lha dang po byung ba gang yin pa de dag go /'di ni sems
5b6(mdo 'grel): can gyi gnas gnyis pa'o/ /sems can gzugs yod pa lus gcig la 'du shes tha dad pa dag yod de/ 'di lta ste/ 'od gsal gyi lha rnams so/ /'di ni sems can gyi gnas gsum pa'o/ /sems can gzugs yod pa lus gcig
5b7(mdo 'grel): cing 'du shes gcig pa dag yod de/ 'di lta ste/ dge rgyas kyi lha rnams so/ /'di ni sems can gyi gnas bzhi pa'o/ /sems can gzugs yod pa 'du shes med cing 'du shes dang bral ba dag yod de/ 'di lta ste/ 'du shes med pa'i lha rnams
6a1(mdo 'grel): so/ /'di ni sems can gyi gnas lnga pa'o/ /sems can gzugs med pa rnam pa thams cad du gzugs kyi 'du shes rnams las yang dag par 'das te/ thogs pa'i 'du shes rnams nub par gyur cing sna tshogs kyi 'du
6a2(mdo 'grel): shes rnams yid la mi byed pas nam mkha' mdza' yas so snyam nas nam mkha' mdza' yas skye mched rdzogs par byas te gnas pa dag yod do/ /'di lta ste/ nam mkha' mdza' yas skye mched du skyes pa'i lha rnams so/ /'di ni sems can gyi gnas
6a3(mdo 'grel): drug pa'o/ /sems can gzugs med pa rnam pa thams cad du nam mkha' mdza' yas skye mched las yang dag par 'das te/ rnam par shes pa mdza' yas so snyam nas rnam shes mdza' yas skye mched rdzogs par byas te gnas pa dag yod de/
6a4(mdo 'grel): 'di lta ste/ rnam shes mdza' yas skye mched du skyes pa'i lha rnams so/ /'di ni sems can gyi gnas bdun pa'o/ /sems can gzugs med pa gang dag rnam pa thams cad du rnam shes mdza' yas skye mched las yang dag par 'das te/ ci yang
6a5(mdo 'grel): med do snyam nas ci yang med pa'i skye mched rdzogs par byas te/ gnas pa dag yod de/ 'di lta ste/ ci yang med pa'i skye mched du skyes pa'i lha rnams so/ /'di ni sems can gyi gnas brgyad pa'o/ /sems can gzugs med pa rnam pa thams
6a6(mdo 'grel): cad du ci yang med pa'i skye mched las yang dag par 'das nas 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched rdzogs par byas te/ gnas pa dag yod de/ 'di lta ste/ 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched du skyes pa'i lha rnams so/ /
6a7(mdo 'grel): 'di ni sems can gyi gnas dgu pa'o/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten khams na/ mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam dag yod de/ srog gcod pa dang/ ma byin par len pa dang/ 'dod pa la log par g.yem pa dang/ brdzun du smra ba dang/ phra
6b1(mdo 'grel): ma dang/ tshig tsub po dang/ tshig 'khyal pa dang/ brnab sems dang/ gnod sems dang/ log par lta ba rnams so/ /srog gcod pa shas chen kun tu bsten cing bsgoms te/ lan mang du byas pas ni sems can dmyal ba chen po mnar ?
6b2(mdo 'grel): skye bar 'gyur ro/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni rab tu tsha bar ro/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni tsha par ro/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni ngu 'bod chen por ro/ de
6b3(mdo 'grel): bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni ngu 'bod du'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni bsdus gzhom du'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni thig nag du'o/ /de bas ches shas chung
6b4(mdo 'grel): ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni sems can dmyal ba chen po yang sos su skye bar 'gyur ro/ /ma byin par len pa shas ches kun tu brten cing bsgoms te/ lan mang du byas pa dang/ 'dod pa la log par g.yem pa dang/ brdzun du smra ba dang/
6b5(mdo 'grel): phra ma dang/ tshig rtsub po dang/ tshig 'khyal pa dang/ brnab sems dang/ gnod sems dang/ log par lta ba shas cher kun du bstan cing bsgoms te/ lan mang du byas pas ni sems can dmyal ba chen po mnar med par skye bar 'gyur ro//
6b6(mdo 'grel): de bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni rab tu che bar ro/ /de bas shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni cha bar ro/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni ngu 'bod chen por ro/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang/
6b7(mdo 'grel): de bas ches yang bas ni ngu 'bod du'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni bsdus gzhom du'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni thig nag du'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni
7a1(mdo 'grel): sems can dmyal ba chen po yang sos su skye bar 'gyur ro/ /'jig rten bzhag pa las tshigs gnyis pa'o/ /mdo la/ mkha' lding las lam bcu po dang/ myong ba dang ni bkres dang zas/ /bdud rtsi phyis char ba dang/ /mu
7a2(mdo 'grel): ge bde dang bcu tshon no/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na klu'i rigs bzhi stong rgya mtsho chen po na gnas so/ /nam mkha' lding gi rigs bzhi stong shing shal ma li mthon po la gnas te/ /sgo nga las skye ba stong dang/ mngal nas skye ba stong
7a3(mdo 'grel): dang/ drod gsher las skye ba stong dang/ rdzus te skye ba stong rnams so/ /nam mkha' lding sgo nga las skye ba'i bza' ba'i phyir klu sgo nga las skye ba 'byin par byed de/ mngal nas skye ba ma yin/ drod gsher las skye ba ma yin/ rdzus te skye ba ma
7a4(mdo 'grel): yin no/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ci te de len na/ de nyid thal ba bzhin du byed par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/ /nam mkha' lding mngal nas skyes pa ni bza' ba'i phyir klu sgo nga las skye ba dang/ mngal nas skye ba 'byin par byed de/ drod gsher las skye ba ma yin
7a5(mdo 'grel): no/ /rdzus te skye ba ma yin no/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ci ste de len na/ de nyid thal ba bzhin du byed par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/ /nam mkha' lding drod gsher las skye ba ni bza' ba'i phyir klu sgo nga las skye ba dang/ mngal nas skye ba dang/ drod gsher las
7a6(mdo 'grel): skye ba 'byin par byed de/ rdzus te skye ba ma yin no/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ci ste de len na de nyid thal ba bzhin du byad par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/ /nam mkha' lding rdzus te skye ba ni bza' ba'i phyir klu sgo nga las skye ba dang/ mngal nas skye ba dang/ drod gsher
7a7(mdo 'grel): las skye ba dang/ rdzus te skye ba 'byin par byed do/ /klu la klu chen po bskal par gnas shings 'dzin pa dag yod do/ /de dag kyang gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ klu'i rgyal po dga' bo dang/ nye dga' gnyis dang/ klu'i rgyal po rtas rgyal dang/ klu'i rgyal
7b1(mdo 'grel): po btang bzung dang/ klu'i rgyal po gzi can dang/ klu'i rgyal po yul 'khor srung dang/ klu'i rgyal po nag po chen po dang/ klu'i rgyal po e la'i 'dab ma rnams te/ 'di dag gzhan yang klu chen po bskal par gnas shings 'dzin pa nam mkha' lding dag gis
7b2(mdo 'grel): dbyung bar mi nus pa gang yin pa 'di dag ni lha dang lha ma yin gyi g.yul myong bar byed cing so sor myong bar byed de/ shes shing rab tu shes la/ kun tu rab tu shes so/ /ji skad du/ shin tu mthu che ba'i klu dag yod do/ ma mdza' srung zhing chu na
7b3(mdo 'grel): gnas pa ste/ /de dag lha min dag dang g.yul 'gyed pas/ 'di dag brgya byin gyis ni dpung yang yin/ /stobs kyang che zhing dug che klu yin te/ /shin tu drag po dgra thabs sna tshogs can/ lha min rnams dang lhan cig g.yul 'gyed pas/ de dag
7b4(mdo 'grel): brgya byin gyis ni dpung yang yin zhes kyang bya'o/ /bar gyi mdo la/ dga' bo nyer dga' rtas rgyal dang/ btang zung dang ni gzi can dang/ /yul 'khor srung dang nag po che/ e la'i 'dab ma phyi ma yin/ stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na dge
7b5(mdo 'grel): ba bcu'i las kyi lam dag yod de/ srog gcod pa spong ba dang/ ma byin par len pa dang/ 'dod pa la log par g.yem pa dang/ brdzun du smra ba dang/ phra ma dang/ tshig rtsub po dang/ tshig 'khyal ba spong ba dang/ brnab sems med pa dang/ gnod sems
7b6(mdo 'grel): med pa dang/ yang dag par lta ba rnams so/ /srog gcod pa spong ba shas cher kun tu bsten cing bsgoms te lan mang du byas pas ni gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams dang skal pa mnyam par skye bar 'gyur ro/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang de bas ches
7b7(mdo 'grel): yang bas ni 'phrul dga' ba rnams su'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni dga' ldan pa rnams su'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni 'thab bral ba rnams su'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang/
8a1(mdo 'grel): de bas ches yang bas ni sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams su'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni rgyal chen bzhi pa rnams su'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas na mi rnams
8a2(mdo 'grel): dang skal ba mnyam par skye bar 'gyur ro/ /ma byin par len pa dang/ 'dod pa log par g.yem pa dang/ brdzun du smra ba dang/ phra ma dang/ tshig rtsub po dang/ tshig 'khyal pa spong ba dang/ chags sems med pa dang/ gnod sems med pa dang/ yang dag par
8a3(mdo 'grel): lta ba shas cher kun tu bsten cing bsgoms te lan mang du byas pas ni gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye bar 'gyur ro/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni 'phrul dga' rnams su'o/ /de bas ches
8a4(mdo 'grel): shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas dga' ldan rnams su'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni 'thab bral ba rnams su'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams su'o/ /de
8a5(mdo 'grel): bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni rgyal chen bzhi pa rnams su'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang/ de bas ches yang bas ni mi rnams dang skal pa mnyam par skye bar 'gyur ro/ /ji ste mi rnams dang skal pa mnyam par skye na
8a6(mdo 'grel): yang sreg gcod pa spong bas ni tshe ring por 'gyur ro/ /ma byin par len pa spong bas ni longs spyod chen por 'gyur ro/ /'dod pa la log par g.yem pa spong bas ni chung ma 'gran zla med par 'gyur ro/ /brdzun du smra ba spong bas ni skur ba mang bar mi 'gyur ro/ /phra ma spong bas ni mdza' ba dang
8a7(mdo 'grel): 'bye bar mi 'gyur ro/ /tshig rtsub po spong bas ni yid du mi 'ong ba'i sgra thos par mi 'gyur ro/ /tshig 'khyal pa spong bas ni tshig mnyam par 'gyur ro/ /chags sems med pas ni 'dod chags che bar mi 'gyur ro/ /gnod sems med pas ni zhe sdang che bar mi 'gyur
8b1(mdo 'grel): ro/ /yang dag pa'i lta bas ni gti mug che bar mi 'gyur ro/ /sems can dmyal bar myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas mnar med pa'i sems can dmyal ba chen po'i che'i tshad bskal par len pa 'di mchog yin no/ /dud
8b2(mdo 'grel): 'gro myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas sa srung gi bus sa srung gi bu nyid dang/ rab tu brtan pas rab tu brtan pa nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no/ /yi dags kyi skye gnas su skye bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang
8b3(mdo 'grel): gi rnam par smin pas rgyal po gshin rje'i gshin rje'i 'jig rten gyi sems can rnams kyi rgyal srid kyi dbang phyug la dbang byed pa 'di ni mchog yin no/ /mi'i skye gnas myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas nga las nus nga
8b4(mdo 'grel): las nus nyid du thob pa 'di mchog yin na/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i ris myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas rgyal po chen po bzhi rnams rgyal srid kyi dbang phyug la dbang byed pa 'di mchog yin no/ /sum cu rtsa gsum myong
8b5(mdo 'grel): par 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pa brgya byin gyis brgya byin nyid thob pa mchog yin no/ /'thab bral myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas rab 'thab bral gyis rab 'thab bral nyid thob pa
8b6(mdo 'grel): 'di mchog yin no/ /dga' ldan myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas yongs su dga' ldan gyis yongs su dga' ldan nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no/ /'phrul dga' myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang
8b7(mdo 'grel): gis rnam par smin pas rab sprul gyis rab sprul nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no/ /gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas dbang byed kyis dbang byed nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no/ /ji ltar 'dzam
9a1(mdo 'grel): bu'i gling gi mi rnams bkres pa dang/ skom pa yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po rnams dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang/ byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang/ rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang/ sum cu rtsa gsum pa
9a2(mdo 'grel): rnams dang/ 'thab bral pa rnams dang/ dga' ldan pa rnams dang/ 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yang yod do/ /de yan chad la ni bkres pa dang/ skom pa med do/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la
9a3(mdo 'grel): kha zas 'di lta ste/ 'bras chan dang/ zan dang/ phye dang/ sha dang/ rus pa rnams yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams ni ma rmos ma btab pa'i 'bras sA lu'i 'bru
9a4(mdo 'grel): za'o/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i ris kyi lha rnams ni dri za'i zas dang bdud rtsi'i zas za'o/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang/ 'thab bral ba rnams dang/ dga' ldan pa rnams dang/ 'phrul dga' ba rnams
9a5(mdo 'grel): dang/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /de yan chad la ni kham gyi zas med de/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi bdud rtsi ni rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang/ ser po dang/ dmar po dang/ dkar po rnams so/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha
9a6(mdo 'grel): rnams ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang/ 'thab bral ba rnams dang/ dga' ldan pa rnams dang/ 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams dang de bzhin no/ /tshangs ris pa rnams la ni med do/ /de yan chad
9a7(mdo 'grel): la yang med do/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la bshang ba dang gci ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po rnams dang/ nub gyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang/ byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams la yang yod de/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams
9b1(mdo 'grel): la ni med do/ /de yan chad la yang med do/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la char 'bab mkhas pa dang/ char 'bab mi mkhas pa yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po rnams dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan pa
9b2(mdo 'grel): rnams dang/ rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni med do/ /de yan chad la yang med do/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la lo legs pa dang/ mu ge yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po dang/ nub gyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang
9b3(mdo 'grel): gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang/ rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni med do/ /de yan chad la yang med do/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la 'jigs pa dang/ bde ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang/ nub gyi ba lang spyod pa rnams
9b4(mdo 'grel): la yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams la ni med do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang/ sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang/ 'thab bral ba rnams dang/ dga' ldan pa rnams dang/ 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la
9b5(mdo 'grel): yod do/ /tshangs ris pa rnams la ni med do/ /de yan chad la yang med do/ /'jig rten bzhag pa las tshigs gsum pa'o// //mdo la/ nyo tshong mdog dang khang pa dang/ /gding ba dang ni bzhag gos dang/ /yang ba rdul rab sgre ba dang/ /tha dad
9b6(mdo 'grel): bag sma len dang bcu/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la nor ram/ 'bru 'am/ gser ram dngul nyo tshong bya ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi
9b7(mdo 'grel): rnams dang/ rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni med do/ /de yan chad la yang med do/ /'di snyam du/ 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams ni nor dang 'bru rnams kyis nyo tshong byed do/ /shar gyi lus 'phags po rnams ni ras dang be'u ras rnams
10a1(mdo 'grel): kyis so/ /nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams ni ba lang dang nor bu rnams kyis so zhes zer ba yod do/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams kyi mdog nag po dang/ /dkar po dang/ sngo bsangs dang/ mdog skya snar
10a2(mdo 'grel): rnam pa bzhi yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams ni mdog gcig pa ste dkar po'o/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi mdog ni rnam pa bzhi'o//
10a3(mdo 'grel): sngon po dang/ ser po dang/ dkar po dang/ dmar po rnams so/ /rgyal chen bzhi po rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang/ 'thab bral ba rnams dang/ dga' ldan pa rnams dang/ 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang/
10a4(mdo 'grel): gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams dang mdog gcig pa ste dkar po'o/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ji lta bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang/ tshangs pa chen po ba rnams dang/ 'od chung ba
10a5(mdo 'grel): rnams dang/ tshad med 'od pa rnams dang/ 'od gsal ba rnams dang/ dge chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med dge ba rnams dang/ dge rgyas pa rnams dang/ sprin med pa rnams dang/ bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang/ 'bras bu che ba rnams dang/
10a6(mdo 'grel): mi che ba rnams dang/ mi gdung ba rnams dang/ gya nom snang ba rnams dang/ shin tu mthong ba rnams dang/ 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /nam mkha' mdza' yas skye mched dang/ rnam shes mdza' yas skye mched dang/ ci yang med
10a7(mdo 'grel): pa'i phyir skye mched dang/ 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched la ni kha dog med do/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams kyi khang pa ched du byas pa dang/ tshad du byas pa ma yin pa dang/ khang bzangs dang/ sa khang rnams yod pa bzhin
10b1(mdo 'grel): du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams kyi khang pa ni ched du byas pa ma yin pa'i sa khang ngo/ /rgyal chen bzhi pa rnams kyi gzhal med khang ni ched du byas pa dang ched du byas pa ma yin pa'o//
10b2(mdo 'grel): rgyal chen bzhi pa'i lha rnams kyi 'jig rten pa bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang/ 'thab bral ba rnams dang/ dga' ldan pa rnams dang/ 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi yang de bzhin no/ /tshangs ris pa rnams
10b3(mdo 'grel): kyis gzhal med khang rnams ni ched du byas pa ma yin pa'o/ /tshangs ris pa rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa dang/ tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang/ 'od chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med 'od pa rnams dang/ 'od gsal ba rnams
10b4(mdo 'grel): dang/ dge chung rnams dang/ tshad med dge ba rnams dang/ dge rgyas pa rnams dang/ sprin med pa rnams dang/ bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang/ 'bras bu che ba rnams dang/ mi che ba rnams dang/ mi gdung ba rnams dang/ gya nom snang ba rnams dang/
10b5(mdo 'grel): shin tu mthong ba rnams dang/ 'og min pa rnams kyi gzhal med khang yang ched du byas pa ma yin no/ /gzugs med pa rnams la ni khang pa med pa'o/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la gding ba dang bgo ba 'di lta ste/ bal gos dang/ sha na'i
10b6(mdo 'grel): ras dang/ gso ma'i ras dang/ zar ma'i ras dang/ ras gos dang/ zab dar dang/ go tam pa'i ras dang/ rtswa du go la'i gos dang/ a pa ran+ti ka'i gos dang/ ras dang/ be'u ras yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang/ nub kyi ba lang
10b7(mdo 'grel): spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams ni dpag bsam shing las byung pa'i gos gyon no/ /ji ltar byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos gyon pa bzhin du rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang/ sum
11a1(mdo 'grel): cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang/ 'thab bral ba rnams dang/ dga' ldan pa rnams dang/ 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ni gos gyon bzhin du skye'o/ /
11a2(mdo 'grel): tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang/ tshangs pa chen po ba rnams dang/ 'od chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med 'od ba rnams dang/ 'od gsal ba rnams dang/ dge chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med dge rnams dang/
11a3(mdo 'grel): dge rgyas pa rnams dang/ sprin med pa rnams dang/ bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang/ 'bras bu che ba rnams dang/ mi che ba rnams dang/ mi gdung ba rnams dang/ gya nom snang ba rnams dang/ shin tu mthong ba rnams dang/ 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang
11a4(mdo 'grel): de gos gyon bzhin du skye'o/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams kyi dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos kyi shing ni rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang/ ser po dang/ dmar po dang/ dkar po rnams so/ /bzhag gos rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang/ ser po dang/
11a5(mdo 'grel): dmar po dang/ dkar po rnams so/ /dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos kyang rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang/ ser po dang/ dmar po dang/ dkar po rnams so/ /dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos ji lta bu 'dod pa de lta bu skyes pa 'am/
11a6(mdo 'grel): bud med dag gi sems bskyed ma thag tu de la yal ga 'dud par byed do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos kyi shing rnams kyang rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang/ ser po dang/ dmar po dang/ dkar po rnams so//
11a7(mdo 'grel): bzhag gos kyang rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang/ ser po dang/ dmar po dang/ dkar po rnams so/ /dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos kyang rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang/ ser po dang/ dmar po dang/ dkar po rnams te/ dpag bsam shing las
11b1(mdo 'grel): byung ba'i gos ji lta bu 'dod pa de lta bu lha'i bu 'am/ lha'i bu mo dag gi sems bskyed ma thag tu yal ga gdung par byed de/ de'i lag tu 'ong bar 'gyur ro/ /rgyal chen bzhi pa rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa dang/ 'thab bral ba rnams dang/
11b2(mdo 'grel): dga' ldan pa rnams dang/ 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi yang de bzhin no/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos med do/ /de yan chad la yang med do/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi
11b3(mdo 'grel): rnams la gding ba dang/ bgo ba lca ba dang/ yang ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams kyi dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos la srang gcig yod do//
11b4(mdo 'grel): rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi ni srang phyed do/ /sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi ni srang gi bzhi cha gcig go /'thab bral ba rnams kyi ni srang gang gi brgyad cha gcig go /dga' ldan pa rnams kyi ni srang gi bcu drug cha gcig go /'phrul dga' ba rnams
11b5(mdo 'grel): kyi sum cu rtsa gnyis kyi srang gi cha gcig go /gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi dpag bsam gyi shing las byung ba'i gos ni srang gi drug cu rtsa bzhi'i cha gcig las med do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams kyi ni gzhal du med pa'i gos yin no/ /tshangs
11b6(mdo 'grel): ris pa rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i 'dun na 'don pa rnams dang/ tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang/ 'od chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med 'od pa rnams dang/ 'od gsal ba rnams dang/ dge chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med dge ba rnams dang/
11b7(mdo 'grel): dge rgyas pa rnams dang/ sprin med pa rnams dang/ bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang/ 'bras bu che ba rnams dang/ mi che ba rnams dang/ mi gdung ba rnams dang/ gya nom snang ba rnams dang/ shin tu mthong ba rnams dang/ 'og min lha rnams kyi yang
12a1(mdo 'grel): gzhal du med pa'i gos yin no/ /nyi zer gyi rdul bzhi bcu rtsa dgu'i cha gcig ni rdul phra rab yin no/ /rdul phra rab bdun ni rdul phra mo gcig go /rdul phra mo bdun la ni nyi zer gyi rdul gcig go /nyi zer gyi rdul bdun la ni
12a2(mdo 'grel): ri bong gi rdul gcig go /ri bong gi rdul bdun la ni lug rdul gcig go /lug rdul bdun la ni glang rdul gcig go /glang rdul bdun la ni sro ma gcig go /sro ma bdun la ni a ba ga na gcig go /a ba ga na gcig la ni ba ti ka gcig go /
12a3(mdo 'grel): ba ti ka bdun la ni nas 'bru gcig go /nas 'bru bdun la ni sor gcig go /sor nyi shu rtsa bzhi la ni khru gang ngo/ /'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams kha cig ni khru tshad de ltar brtsis pa'i khru phyed dang bzhi pa'o/ /kha cig ni khru bzhi pa'o/ /shar
12a4(mdo 'grel): gyi lus 'phags pa rnams ni khru brgyad pa'o/ /nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams ni khru bcu drug pa'o/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams ni khru sum cu rtsa gnyis pa'o/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi lus thob pa ni rgyang grags kyi bzhi cha gcig
12a5(mdo 'grel): go /sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams kyi ni rgyang grags kyi phyed do/ /'thab bral ba rnams kyi ni rgyang grags kyi bzhi cha gsum mo/ /dga' ldan pa rnams kyi ni rgyang grags gcig go /'phrul dga' ba rnams rgyang grags gcig dang/ rgyang grags
12a6(mdo 'grel): kyi bzhi cha gcig go /gzhan 'phrul dbang byed rnams kyi ni rgyang grags phyed dang gnyis so/ /tshangs ris pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad phyed do/ /tshangs pa mdun na 'don pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad gcig go /tshangs pa chen po pa rnams kyi ni
12a7(mdo 'grel): dpag tshad phyed dang gnyis so/ /'od chung ba rnams kyi ni dpag tshad gnyis so/ /tshad med nyon pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad bzhi po/ /'od gsal ba rnams kyi ni dpag tshad brgyad do/ /dge chung ba rnams kyi ni dpag tshad bcu drug go /tshad
12b1(mdo 'grel): med dge ba rnams kyi ni dpag tshad sum cu rtsa gnyis so/ /dge rgyas pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad drug cu rtsa bzhi'o/ /sprin med pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad brgya nyi shu rtsa lnga'o/ /bsod nams skyes pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad nyis brgya lnga bcu'o/ /'bras
12b2(mdo 'grel): bu che ba'i lha rnams kyi ni dpag tshad lnga brgya'o/ /'du shes med pa'i sems can rnams kyi yang de dang 'dra'o/ mi che ba'i lus thob pa ni dpag tshad stong ngo/ /mi gdung ba rnams kyi dpag tshad nyis stong ngo/ /gya nom snang ba rnams kyi ni dpag tshad bzhi
12b3(mdo 'grel): stong ngo/ /shin tu mthong ba pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad brgyad stong ngo/ /'og min gyi lha rnams kyi lus thob pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad khri drug stong ngo/ /gzugs med pa rnams la ni bsags pa'i lus med do/ /nyi zer gyi rdul bzhi bcu rtsa
12b4(mdo 'grel): dgu'i cha gcig gi ni rdul phra rab yin no/ /rdul phra rab bdun la ni rdul phra mo gcig go /rdul phra mo bdun la ni nyi zer gyi rdul gcig go /nye zer gyi rdul bdun la ni ri bong gi rdul gcig go /ri bong gi rdul bdun la ni lug rdul gcig go /lug
12b5(mdo 'grel): rdul bdun la ni glang rdul gcig go /glang rdul bdun la ni sro ma gcig go /sro ma bdun la ni a ba gan gcig go /a ba ga na bdun la ni ba ti ka gcig go /ba ti ka bdun la ni nas 'bru gcig go /nas 'bru bdun la ni sor gcig go /
12b6(mdo 'grel): sor nyi shu rtsa bzhi la khru gang ngo/ /'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams kha cig gos khru tshad 'di lta bur brtsis pa'i khru brgyad pa gyon no/ /kha cig ni khru bcu pa'o/ /shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams kyi khru nyi shu pa'o/ /nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams kyi
12b7(mdo 'grel): ni khru bzhi bcu pa'o/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams kyi ni dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos khru brgyad cu pa gyon gyon no/ /rgyal chen bzhi pa'i lha rnams kyang lus la ci ran pa'i gos gyon no/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi ji lta ba
13a1(mdo 'grel): bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang/ 'thab bral ba rnams dang/ dga' ldan pa rnams dang/ 'phrul dgal pa rnams dang/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams dang/ tshangs ris pa rnams dang/ tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don
13a2(mdo 'grel): pa rnams dang/ tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang/ 'od chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med 'od pa rnams dang/ 'od gsal ba rnams dang/ dge chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med dge ba rnams dang/ dge rgyas pa rnams dang/ sprin med pa rnams dang/ bsod
13a3(mdo 'grel): nams skyes pa rnams dang/ 'bras bu che ba rnams dang/ mi che ba rnams dang/ mi gdung ba rnams dang/ gya nom snang ba rnams dang/ shin tu mthong ba rnams dang/ 'og min pa rnams kyi yang de bzhin no/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi
13a4(mdo 'grel): rnams dbang po tha dad do/ /kha cig la ni mo'i dbang po dang/ kha cig la ni pho'i dbang po yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang/ byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang/ rgyal chen bzhi pa'i lha
13a5(mdo 'grel): rnams dang/ sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams dang/ 'thab bral ba rnams dang/ dga' ldan pa rnams dang/ 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yang yod do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni mo'i dbang po
13a6(mdo 'grel): yang med/ pho'i dbang po yang med do/ /tshangs ris pa rnams ji lta ba bzhin du/ tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang/ tshangs pa chen po rnams dang/ 'od chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med 'od pa rnams dang/ 'od gsal ba rnams dang/
13a7(mdo 'grel): dge chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med dge ba rnams dang/ dge rgyas pa rnams dang/ sprin med pa rnams dang/ bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang/ 'bras bu che ba rnams dang/ mi che ba rnams dang/ mi gdud pa rnams dang/ gya nom snang ba rnams
13b1(mdo 'grel): dang/ shin tu mthong ba rnams dang/ 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la bag ma gtong ba dang/ bag ma len pa yod pa bzhin du/ shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang/ nub kyi ba lang
13b2(mdo 'grel): spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams la ni med do/ /rgyal chen bzhi pa'i lha rnams dang/ sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang/ 'thab bral ba rnams dang/ dga' ldan pa rnams dang/ 'phrul dga' 
13b3(mdo 'grel): ba rnams dang/ /gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yang yod do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni bag ma gtong ba yang med len pa yang med do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams
13b4(mdo 'grel): dang/ tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang/ 'od chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med 'od pa rnams dang/ 'od gsal ba rnams dang/ dge chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med dge ba rnams dang/ dge rgyas pa rnams dang/ sprin med pa rnams
13b5(mdo 'grel): dang/ bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang/ 'bras bu che ba rnams dang/ mi che ba rnams dang/ mi gdung ba rnams dang/ gya nom snang ba rnams dang/ shin tu mthong ba rnams dang/ 'og min gyi lha rnams la yang de bzhin no/ /
13b6(mdo 'grel): 'jig rten bzhag pa las tshigs bzhi pa'o/ /'jig rten bzhag pa// //bam po gnyis pa/ mdo la/ grang dang tsha dang dus tshigs mtshan mo dang/ pha ma dang ni rje khol dang/ /nor dang 'bru dang mngon par zhe na/ /bcu
13b7(mdo 'grel): tshan yongs su brjod pa yin/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la shin tu grang ba dang/ shin tu tsha ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi
14a1(mdo 'grel): snyan pa rnams la ni med do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la yang med do/ /de yan chad la yang med do/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la dus tshigs 'di lta ste/ dgun dang/ dpyid dang/ dbyar
14a2(mdo 'grel): yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang/ byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang/ rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang/ sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang/ 'thab bral ba rnams dang/
14a3(mdo 'grel): dga' ldan pa rnams dang/ 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams la yang yod do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni dus tshigs med do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na
14a4(mdo 'grel): 'don pa rnams dang/ tshangs pa chen po rnams dang/ 'od chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med 'od pa rnams dang/ 'od gsal ba rnams dang/ dge chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med dge ba rnams dang/ dge rgyas pa rnams dang/ sprin med pa
14a5(mdo 'grel): rnams dang/ bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang/ 'bras bu che ba rnams dang/ mi che ba rnams dang/ mi gdung ba rnams dang/ gya nom snang ba rnams dang/ shin tu mthong ba rnams dang/ 'og min gyi lha rnams la yang de bzhin no/ /ji
14a6(mdo 'grel): ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la mtshan mo dang/ nyin mo yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang/ byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang/ rgyal chen bzhi'i lha dang/ sum cu rtsa gsum
14a7(mdo 'grel): pa rnams dang/ 'thab bral ba rnams dang/ dga' ldan pa rnams dang/ 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams yang yod do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni mtshan mo yang med/ nyin mo yang med do/ /
14b1(mdo 'grel): tshangs ris pa rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang/ tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang/ 'od chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med 'od pa rnams dang/ 'od gsal ba rnams
14b2(mdo 'grel): dang/ dge chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med dge pa rnams dang/ dge rgyas pa rnams dang/ sprin med pa rnams dang/ bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang/ 'bras bu che ba rnams dang/ mi che ba rnams dang/ mi gdung ba rnams dang/ gya nom snang ba rnams dang/ shin tu mthong ba rnams dang/ 'og
14b3(mdo 'grel): min gyi lha rnams la yang de bzhin no/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la pha dang ma yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang/ byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang/ rgyal chen bzhi'i
14b4(mdo 'grel): lha rnams dang/ sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang/ 'thab bral ba rnams dang/ dga' ldan pa rnams dang/ 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams la yang yod do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni ma yang med
14b5(mdo 'grel): pha yang med do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang/ tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang/ 'od chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med 'od pa rnams dang/ 'od gsal ba rnams dang/ dge chung ba rnams
14b6(mdo 'grel): dang/ tshad med dge ba rnams dang/ dge rgyas pa rnams dang/ sprin med pa rnams dang/ bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang/ 'bras bu che ba rnams dang/ mi che ba rnams dang/ mi gdung ba rnams dang/ gya nom snang ba rnams dang/ shin tu
14b7(mdo 'grel): mthong ba rnams dang/ 'og min gyi lha rnams la yang de bzhin no/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la rje bo dang bran yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra
15a1(mdo 'grel): mi snyan pa rnams la ni rje bo dang bran kyang yod do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni rje bo dang bran kyang yod do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang/ 'thab bral ba rnams dang/ dga' 
15a2(mdo 'grel): ldan pa rnams dang/ 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yang de bzhin no/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni rje bo yang med bran yang med do/ /tshangs ris pa rnams la ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don
15a3(mdo 'grel): pa rnams dang/ tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang/ 'od chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med 'od pa rnams dang/ 'od gsal ba rnams dang/ dge chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med dge ba rnams dang/ dge rgyas pa rnams dang/ sprin med pa rnams
15a4(mdo 'grel): dang/ bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang/ 'bras bu che ba rnams dang/ mi che ba rnams dang/ mi gdung ba rnams dang/ gya nom snang ba rnams dang/ shin tu mthong ba rnams dang/ 'og min gyi lha rnams la yang de bzhin no/ /ji ltar
15a5(mdo 'grel): 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la nor dang/ 'bru yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams la ni 'bru ni yod nor ni med do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i
15a6(mdo 'grel): lha rnams la ni nor ni yod la 'bru ni med do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang/ 'thab bral ba rnams dang/ dga' ldan pa rnams dang/ 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang/ gzhan 'phrul dbang
15a7(mdo 'grel): byed pa rnams la yang de bzhin no/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni nor yang med 'bru yang med do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa mdun na 'don pa rnams dang/ tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang/ 'od chung ba rnams dang/ tshad
15b1(mdo 'grel): med 'od pa rnams dang/ 'od gsal ba rnams dang/ dge chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med dge ba rnams dang/ dge rgyas pa rnams dang/ sprin med pa rnams dang/ bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang/ 'bras bu che ba rnams dang/ mi che ba rnams dang/
15b2(mdo 'grel): mi gdung ba rnams dang/ gya nom snang ba rnams dang/ shin tu mthong ba rnams dang/ 'og min gyi lha rnams la yang de bzhin no/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la pha 'am ma 'am/ bu pho 'am bu mo 'am/ rje bo 'am/ bran nam/ nor ram/
15b3(mdo 'grel): 'bru la mngon par zhen pa yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams la ni ci la'ang mngon par zhen pa med do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni
15b4(mdo 'grel): 'bru ma gtogs pa rnams la mngon par zhen pa yod do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang/ 'thab bral ba rnams dang/ dga' ldan pa rnams dang/ 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang/ gzhan
15b5(mdo 'grel): 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi yang de bzhin no/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la yang mngon par zhen pa med do/ /tshangs ris pa rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang/ tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang/ 'od
15b6(mdo 'grel): chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med 'od pa rnams dang/ 'od gsal ba rnams dang/ dge chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med dge ba rnams dang/ dge rgyas pa rnams dang/ sprin med pa rnams dang/ bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang/ 'bras
15b7(mdo 'grel): bu che ba rnams dang/ mi che ba rnams dang/ mi gdung ba rnams dang/ gya nom snang ba rnams dang/ shin tu mthong ba rnams dang/ 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /'jig rten bzhag pa las tshigs lnga pa'o// //
16a1(mdo 'grel): mdo la/ zla mtshan 'khrig dang khu chu dang/ /tshe bsgyur dang ni chu klung brag /sa la rdzing bu glang po dang/ /srungs ma 'khor los sgyur ba'i lam/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la bud med zla mtshan
16a2(mdo 'grel): can dang/ sbrum ma dang/ bu btsa' ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang/ byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams la yang yod do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi ni 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi
16a3(mdo 'grel): rnams kyi khye'u 'am/ bu mo lo lnga lon pa ji tsam pa de bzhin no/ /lha 'am lha'i bu mo'i phrag pa 'am phang bar sems can brdzus te skye bar 'gyur te/ de la lha 'am lha'i bu mo dag 'di snyam du 'di ni bdag gi bu 'am bu mo snyam du
16a4(mdo 'grel): sems so/ /khye'u dang bu mo de dag kyang 'di snyam du 'di ni bdag cag gi ma 'am pha'o snyam du sems so/ /sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams kyi ni lo drug lon pa ji tsam pa bzhin no/ /'thab bral ba rnams kyi ni lo bdun lon pa ji
16a5(mdo 'grel): tsam pa bzhin no/ /dga' ldan pa rnams kyi ni lo brgyad lon pa ji tsam pa bzhin no/ /'phrul dga' ba rnams kyi ni lo dgu lon pa ji tsam pa bzhin no/ /gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi ni 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams kyi khye'u
16a6(mdo 'grel): dang bu mo lo bcu lon pa ji tsam pa de bzhin du lha 'am lha'i bu mo'i phrag pa 'am phang par brdzus te skye ba'i sems can 'byung bar 'gyur te/ de na lha 'am lha'i bu mo dag 'di snyam du 'di ni bdag gi bu 'am bu mo snyam du sems so/
16a7(mdo 'grel): khye'u dang bu mo de dag kyang 'di snyam du 'di ni bdag cag gi ma 'am pha'o snyam du sems so/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ni thog ma nas lus kyi yan lag dang nying lag thams cad rdzogs par skye zhing 'chi ba na yang de kho na nyid do/ /
16b1(mdo 'grel): tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang/ tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang/ 'od chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med 'od pa rnams dang/ 'od gsal ba rnams dang/ dge chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med dge ba rnams 
16b2(mdo 'grel): dang/ dge rgyas pa rnams dang/ sprin med pa rnams dang/ bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang/ 'bras bu che ba rnams dang/ mi che ba rnams dang/ mi gdung ba rnams dang/ gya nom snang ba rnams dang/ shin tu mthong ba rnams dang/ 'og
16b3(mdo 'grel): min pa rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /gzugs med pa rnams la ni lus kyi gzugs med de/ de bas na de dag gi skye ba yang mi mngon/ 'chi 'pho ba yang mi mngon no/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams mi tshangs par spyod pa 'khrig
16b4(mdo 'grel): pa'i chos bsten pa na gnyis kyis gnyis sbyor ba bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang/ byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang/ rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang/ sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams
16b5(mdo 'grel): kyang de bzhin no/ /'thab bral ba rnams ni 'khyud pa tsam gyis gdung ba zhi bar 'gyur ro/ /dga' ldan pa rnams kyis ni lag pa nas bzung ba tsam gyis so/ 'phrul dga' ba rnams kyis brgad pa tsam gyis so/ /gzhan 'phrul
16b6(mdo 'grel): dbang byed pa rnams kyi ni bltas pa tsam gyis gdung ba zhi bar 'gyur ro/ /tshangs ris pa rnams la ni 'dod chags med do/ /tshangs ris pa rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang/ tshangs pa chen po pa rnams
16b7(mdo 'grel): dang/ 'od chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med 'od pa rnams dang/ 'od gsal ba rnams dang/ dge chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med dge ba rnams dang/ dge rgyas pa rnams dang/ sprin med pa rnams dang/ bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang/
17a1(mdo 'grel): 'bras bu che ba rnams dang/ mi che ba rnams dang/ mi gdung ba rnams dang/ gya nom snang ba rnams dang/ shin tu mthong ba rnams dang/ 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams
17a2(mdo 'grel): la khu chu mi gtsang ba 'byung ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang/ byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams la yang de bzhin no/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi rlung 'byung ngo/ /rgyal chan
17a3(mdo 'grel): bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang/ 'thab bral ba rnams dang/ dga' ldan pa rnams dang/ 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi yang de bzhin no/ /tshangs ris kyi lha
17a4(mdo 'grel): rnams la ni 'dod chags med do/ /tshangs ris pa rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang/ tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang/ 'od chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med 'od pa rnams dang/ 'od gsal ba rnams dang/
17a5(mdo 'grel): dge chung ba rnams dang/ tshad med dge ba rnams dang/ dge rgyas pa rnams dang/ sprin med pa rnams dang/ bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang/ 'bras bu che ba rnams dang/ mi che ba rnams dang/ mi gdung ba rnams dang/ gya nom snang
17a6(mdo 'grel): ba rnams dang/ shin tu mthong ba rnams dang/ 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /sems can dmyal ba'i sems can gyi tshe'i tshang kyi mdza' ni bskal pa gcig ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /dud 'gro'i skye gnas su skyes
17a7(mdo 'grel): pa'i sems can rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' i skal pa gcig te/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod de/ /mi rnams kyi nyin zhag sum cu gang yin pa de ni yi dags rnams kyi nyin gcig ste/ nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig /zla ba bcu gnyis
17b1(mdo 'grel): la lo gcig ste/ yi dags rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lo lnga brgya ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i steng brtsis na lo khri lnga stong yod do/ /shar gyi lus 'phags kyi mi rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni lo nyis
17b2(mdo 'grel): brgya lnga bcu ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /nub kyi ba lang spyad kyi mi rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni lo lnga brgya ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams kyi tshe'i chad kyi mdza' ni lo stong ste/ bar ma der 'chi ba med
17b3(mdo 'grel): do/ /ci'i phyir byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams ni bar ma dor 'chi ba ni med ce na/ de dag la bdag gi ba med cing yongs su 'dzin pa med de/ tshe nges shing khyad par 'gro ba yin pas/ de'i phyir byang gi sgra mi snyan rnams la bar ma dor 'chi ba med
17b4(mdo 'grel): do/ /'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la yang skye ba dang/ mar 'grib pa yod de/ 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams re 'ga' ni tshe dpag tu med par 'gyur la/ re 'ga' ni tshe lo bcu bar 'gyur ro/ /mi rnams kyi tshe lo lnga bcu gang yin pa de ni/
17b5(mdo 'grel): rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi nyin zhag gcig go/ nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig /zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lha'i lo lnga brgya ste/ bar ma
17b6(mdo 'grel): dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar brtsin? lo sa ya phrag dgu yod do/ /de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po yang sos kyi nyin zhag gcig go/ nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sems can
17b7(mdo 'grel): dmyal? ba yang sos kyi sems can rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni de lo lta bu rab rtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba pa'i lo lnga brgya ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag 'bum drug khri nyis stong yod
18a1(mdo 'grel): do/ /mi rnams kyi lo brgya gang yin pa de ni sum cu rtsa gsum gyi nyin zhag gcig go/ nyin zhag de sum nu la zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sum cu rtsa gsum gyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i
18a2(mdo 'grel): tshad kyi mdza' ni de lta bur brtsis pa'i lha'i lo stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag gsum dang/ sa ya phrag drug yod do/ /de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po thig nag gi nyin zhag gcig
18a3(mdo 'grel): go/ nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sems can dmyal ba chen po thig nag gi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba'i lo stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /
18a4(mdo 'grel): de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag 'bum phrag bcu gnyis dang/ bye ba phrag dgu khri drug stong yod do/ /mi rnams kyi lo nyis brgya gang yin pa de ni 'thab bral gyi lha rnams kyi nyin zhag gcig go/ nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig/ zla
18a5(mdo 'grel): ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste 'thab bral ba'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lha'i lo nyis stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag bcu bzhi dang sa ya phrag bzhi yod do/ /
18a6(mdo 'grel): de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po bsdus gzhom gyi nyin zhag gcig go/ nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sems can dmyal ba chen po bsdus gzhom gyi sems can rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi
18a7(mdo 'grel): mdza' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba'i lo nyis stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar brtsis nas lo bye ba phrag gcig dang/ bya ba phrag gsum 'bum drug khri brgyad stong yod do/ /mi rnams kyi lo bzhi
18b1(mdo 'grel): brgya gang yin pa de ni dga' ldan gyi lha rnams kyi nyin zhag gcig go/ nyin zhag sum cu la zla ba gcig /zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ dga' ldan gyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i la bzhi stong yod do/ /bar ma dor
18b2(mdo 'grel): 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag lnga bcu rtsa bdun dang/ lo sa ya phrag drug yod do/ /de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po du 'bod kyi nyin zhag gcig go /nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig /zla ba bcu gnyis
18b3(mdo 'grel): la lo gcig ste/ sems can dmyal ba chen po ngu 'bod kyi sems can dmyal ba pa'i sems can rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i la bzhi stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo
18b4(mdo 'grel): bye ba phrag bye ba brgyad dang/ byo? ba phrag sa ya gnyis dang/ bye ba phrag dgu 'bum bzhi khri bzhi stong yod do/ /mi rnams kyi lo brgyad brgya gang yin pa de ni 'phrul dga' i lha rnams kyi nyin zhag gcig go /nyin zhag sum cu la zla ba gcig go /zla ba bcu gnyis la lo
18b5(mdo 'grel): gcig ste/ 'phrul dga' i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lha'i lo brgyad stong ste/ bar mdo'i 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag gnyis brgya sum cu dang/ lo sa ya phrag bzhi yod
18b6(mdo 'grel): do/ /de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po ngu 'bod chen po'i nyin zhag gcig go/ nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig /zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sems can dmyal ba chen po ngu 'bod chen po'i tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni lo de lta
18b7(mdo 'grel): bur brtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba'i lo brgyad stong yod de/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag drug cu rtsa drug dang/ bye ba phrag so ya gsum dang/ bye ba phrag lnga 'bum lnga khri nyis stong yod do/ /
19a1(mdo 'grel): mi rnams kyi lo stong drug brgya gang yin pa de ni gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams kyi nyin zhag gcig go /nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi
19a2(mdo 'grel): lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lha'i lo khri drug stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag dgu brgya nyi shu rtsa gcig dang/ lo sa ya phrag drug yod do/ /de ni sems can dmyal ba chen
19a3(mdo 'grel): po che ba'i nyin zhag gcig go/ nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sems can dmyal ba chen po tsha ba'i sems can dmyal ba ba'i sems can rnams kyi tshe'i tshad ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i sems can
19a4(mdo 'grel): dmyal ba pa'i lo khri drug stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar brtsis nas na lo bye ba phrag lnga brgya dang/ lo bye ba phrag bye ba sum cu dang/ lo bye ba phrag sa ya brgyad dang/ bzhi 'bum dang/ lo bye ba phrag khri drug stong yod do//
19a5(mdo 'grel): bar gyi mdo la/ dgu dang gsum dang bcu bzhi dang ni lnga bcu rtsa bdun dang/ nyis brgya dgu brgya rnams ni mi'i grangs kyis lha tsher bshad/ de bzhin gcig bcu gnyis gcig dang brgyad dang drug cu dang/ lnga brgya dag ni sems can dmyal
19a6(mdo 'grel): ba'i tsher bshad do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal ba phyed de/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /sems can dmyal ba chen po rab tu tsha ba'i tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal ba phyed de/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /tshangs
19a7(mdo 'grel): pa'i mdun 'don pa'i lha rnams kyi tshe 'tshed? kyi mdza' ni bskal pa gcig ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /sems can dmyal ba chen po mnar med pa'i tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal pa gcig ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod
19b1(mdo 'grel): do/ /tshangs pa chen po pa'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal pa byed dang nyis te/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /'od chung gi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal pa gnyis te/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /tshad med 'od kyi lha rnams
19b2(mdo 'grel): kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal pa bzhi ste/ bar ma der 'chi ba ni yod do/ /'od gsal gyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal pa brgyad de/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /dge chung gi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal pa bcu
19b3(mdo 'grel): drug ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /tshad med dge ba'i lha rnam kyi che'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal pa sum cu rtsa gnyis te/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /dge rgyas kyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal pa drug cu rtsa bzhi ste/
19b4(mdo 'grel): bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /sprin med kyi lha rnam kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal pa brgya? nyi shu rtsa lnga ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /bsod nams skyes kyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal pa nyis brgya lnga bcu ste/ bar ma
19b5(mdo 'grel): dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /'bras bu che ba'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal pa lnga brgya ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /'du shes med pa'i sems can rnams de 'dra'o/ /mi che ba'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal pa stong ste/
19b6(mdo 'grel): bar ma der 'chi ba ni yod do/ mi gdung ba'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal pa nyis stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /gya nom snang ba'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal pa bzhi stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/
19b7(mdo 'grel): shin tu mthong ba'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal pa brgyad stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /'og min gyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal pa khri drug stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /nam mkha' mdza' yas
20a1(mdo 'grel): skye mched pa'i tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal pa nyi khri ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /rnam shes mdza' yas skye mched pa'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshang? kyi mdza' ni bskal pa bzhi khri ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /ci yang med
20a2(mdo 'grel): pa'i skye mched kyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal pa drug khri ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched pa'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mdza' ni bskal pa brgyad khri ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /'di
20a3(mdo 'grel): nas byang phyogs na ri nag po gsum yod do/ /ri nag po gsum po de dag gi byang phyogs na ri nag po gzhan gsum yod do/ /ri nag po gzhan gsum po de dag gi byang phyogs na ri'i rgyal po gangs zhes bya ba yod do/ /ri'i rgyal po gangs
20a4(mdo 'grel): kyi byang phyogs na/ ri'i rgyal po spos kyi dang ldan zhes bya ba yod do/ /ri'i rgyal po spos kyi dad ldang nas dpag tshad bcu'i tshul? rol na mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba zhig yod de/ ma dros pa zhes kyang bya'o/ /mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba de la tshur dpag
20a5(mdo 'grel): tshad lnga bcu yod do/ /zhing du dpag tshad lnga bcu yod do/ /mdza' skor du ni dpag tshad nyis brgya yod do/ /dbyibs legs shing lta na sdug la mdzes pa chu bsil zhing chu sprang rtsi lta bus gang la/ me tog utpal dang/ pad+ma dang/ ku mu da
20a6(mdo 'grel): dang/ pad+ma dkar pos kun tu phebs par 'dug go/ de'i nang nas chu klung chen po bzhi 'di lta ste/ gang+gA dang/ sindu dang/ pak+Shu dang/ si ta dang 'di rnams 'bab ste/ gang+ga ni shar phyogs nas glang po che'i kha nas 'bab ste/ mtsho chen
20a7(mdo 'grel): po chu zhes bya ba'i g.yas phyogs su bskor nas/ klung lnga brgya dang lhan cig tu shar phyogs kyi rgya mtsho chen por 'gro'o/ /sindu ni lho phyogs nas khyu mchog gi kha nas 'bab ste/ de ni mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba'i g.yas phyogs su bskor
20b1(mdo 'grel): nas klung lnga brgya dang lhan cig tu lho phyogs kyi rgya mtsho chen por 'gro'o/ /pak+Shu ni nub phyogs nas rta'i kha nas 'bab ste/ de ni mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba'i g.yas phyogs su bskor nas klung lnga brgya dang lhan cig tu nub phyogs kyi rgya mtsho chen por
20b2(mdo 'grel): 'gro'o/ /si ta ni byang phyogs nas seng ge'i kha nas 'bab ste/ de ni mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba'i g.yas phyogs su bskor nas/ klung lnga brgya dang lhan cig tu byang phyogs kyi rgya mtsho chen por 'gro'o/ /'di skad du/ byang phyogs kha dgur 'gyur
20b3(mdo 'grel): ba yi/ /chu mtsho yod de gzhan dag kyang/ /de na mtsho chen chu zhes bya/ /tha dad rgyu rnams 'byung gnas yod/ /chu klung gang+ga sindu pak+Shu dang/ si ta dpa' rlabs dbu ba'i phreng ba can/ /'bab cing thams cad bsil ba'i chu yin te/ /
20b4(mdo 'grel): phyogs bzhi kho ra khor yug dag nas 'byung/ /gang+gA shar phyogs rgya mtshor 'gro ba ste/ sindu lho phyogs rgya mtshor 'gro ba yin/ /pak+Shu yang ni nub phyogs rgya mtshor 'gro/ de'i byang phyogs rgya mtshor si ta 'gro/ chu klung rab mchog
20b5(mdo 'grel): bzhi po 'di dag ni/ /mchog tu bzang zhing so sor 'bab pa ste/ /re re zhing yang lnga brgya khyer nas ni/ /chu'i rgyun rnams rgya mtsho chen por 'gro zhes kyang bya'o/ /ri sbos kyi ngad ldang de'i byang phyogs dpag tshad nyi shu na gser gyi brag
20b6(mdo 'grel): bya skyibs lha ma yin gyi ngos zhes bya ba yod de/ chur dpag tshad lnga bcu zheng du yang dpag tshad lnga bcu/ /mdza' skor du nyis brgya 'phang du dpag tshad phyed dang bzhi yod pa/ dbyibs legs shing lta na sdug la mdzes pa zhig yod
20b7(mdo 'grel): de/ de'i nang gis sa gzhi yang dbyibs legs shing lta na sdug la/ mdzes pa gser gyi phye ma brdal cing tsan dan gyi chus chag chag btab pa ste/ der yid du mi 'ong ba'i shing ngam/ gseg ma 'am/ gang ci yang rung ba dag ltung
21a1(mdo 'grel): na de mi ma yin pa rnams kyis rlung gi mthus phyi rol tu gtor ro/ /de'i khor khor yug na gser gyi brag bya skyibs can brgya stong yod do/ /de dag thams cad kyang legs shing lta na sdug la
21a2(mdo 'grel): mdzes pa ste/ de dag gi nang sa gzhi rnams kyang dbyibs legs shing lta na sdug la/ mdzes pa gser gyi phye ma brdal cing tsan dan gyi chu sa chag chag btab pa ste/ de dag tu 'ang yid du mi 'ong ba shing ngam/ gseg
21a3(mdo 'grel): ma 'am/ gang ci yang rung ba dag ltung na/ de mi ma yin pa rnams kyi rlung gi mthus phyi rol tu 'dor ro/ /de'i lam srid du dpag tshad nyi shu/ zheng du dpag tshad phyed dang gnyis yod pa dbyibs legs lta na sdug la
21a4(mdo 'grel): mdzes pa gser gyi phye ma brdal cing tsan dan gyi chus chag chag btab pa zhig yod de/ de yang yid du mi 'ong ba shing ngam gseg ma 'am/ gang ci yang rung ba dag lhung na nga mi ma yin pa rnams kyis rlung gi mthus phyi
21a5(mdo 'grel): rol du 'dor ro/ /brag bya skyibs lha ma yin gyi ngos de'i byang phyogs dpag tshad nyi shu na shing sA la'i rgyal po chen po rab tu brtan pa zhes bya ba sA la'i phreng ba rim pa bdun gyis bskor ba zhig yod do/ /sA la'i rgyal
21a6(mdo 'grel): po rab tu brtan pa da rtsa ba ni 'dom bcu bzhi thur du zug go /sA la'i phreng ba dang po'i rtsa ba ni 'dom bcu gsum thur du zug go /gnyis pa'i ni bcu gnyis so/ /gsum pa'i bcu gcig go /bzhi pa'i ni bcu'o//
21a7(mdo 'grel): lnga pa'i ni dgu'o/ /drug pa ni brgyad do/ /sA la'i phreng ba bdun pa'i rtsa ba ni 'dom bdun thur du zug go /sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa de'i yal ga dang/ lo ma dang/ yan lag rnams gang yin pa de ni sA
21b1(mdo 'grel): la'i phreng ba dang po la thug go /sA la'i phreng ba dang po ni yal ga dang lo ma dang yan lag gang yin pa de ni gnyis pa la'o/ /gnyis pa'i gang yin pa ni gsum pa la'o/ /gsum pa'i gang yin pa de ni bzhi pa la'o//
21b2(mdo 'grel): bzhi pa'i gang yin pa de ni lnga pa la'o/ /lnga pa'i gang yin pa de ni drug pa la'o/ /drug pa'i gang yin pa de ni bdun pa la'o/ /sA la'i phreng ba bdun pa'i yal ga dang/ lo ma dang yal ga gang yin pa de ni nam mkha' 
21b3(mdo 'grel): khyab par 'dug go /de'i nang gi sa gzhi yang dbyibs legs shing lta na sdug la/ mdzes pa gser gyi phye ma brdal cing tsan dan gyi chus chag chag btab pa ste/ de yang yid du mi 'ong ba shing ngam gseg ma
21b4(mdo 'grel): 'am/ gang ci yang rung ba dag lhung na ni de mi ma yin pa rnams kyis rlung gi mthus phyi rol du 'dor ro/ /de'i lam srid du dpag tshad nyi shu/ zheng du dpag tshad phyed dang gnyis yod pa/ dbyibs legs
21b5(mdo 'grel): shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa zhig yod do/ /der yang yid du mi 'ong ba shing ngam gseg ma 'am gang ci yang rung ba dag ltung na de mi ma yin pa rnams kyis rlung gi mthus phyi rol du 'dor ro/ /sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan
21b6(mdo 'grel): ba'i shar phyogs dpag tshad nyi shu na/ rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab ces bya ba chur dpag tshad lnga bcu/ zheng du yang dpag tshad lnga bcu ste/ mdza' skor du dpag tshad nyis brgya yod pa/ dbyibs legs shing blta na
21b7(mdo 'grel): sdug la mdzes pa chu bsil zhing chu sbrang rtsi lta bus gang ba/ me tog utpa la dang/ pad+ma dang ku mu da dang/ pad+ma dkar pos khebs pa zhig yod de/ rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab/ de'i nang gi pad+ma'i lo ma rnams che zhing
22a1(mdo 'grel): mchog tu che ste/ /'di lta ste/ ba lang gi ko ba tsam mo/ /pad+ma'i sdong bu rnams che zhing mchog tu che ste/ 'di lta ste/ gshol mnga' tsam mo/ /pad+ma'i me tog rnams che zhing mchog tu che ba ste/ 'di
22a2(mdo 'grel): lta ste/ shing rta'i 'phang lo tsam mo/ /pad+ma'i rtsa ba rnams che zhing mchog tu che ste/ 'di lta ste/ skyes bu chen po'i brla tsam mo/ /ro mngar zhing mchog tu mngar ste/ 'di lta ste/ sbrang bu'i sbrang rtsi ma bskol ba bzhin no/ /
22a3(mdo 'grel): bcad na yang 'o ma 'dzag go /rdzing bu dal gyi 'bab gyi khor khor yug na rdzing bu brgyad stong yod de/ de dag thams cad kyang dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa chu bsil zhing sbrang rtsi lta bus gang ngo/ /de
22a4(mdo 'grel): dag gi nang gi pad+ma'i lo ma rnams kyang che zhing mchog tu che ste/ 'di lta ste/ ba lang gi ko ba tsam mo/ /pad+ma'i sdong bu rnams che zhing mchog tu che ste/ 'di lta ste/ gshol mnga' tsam mo/ /pad+ma'i me tog rnams che
22a5(mdo 'grel): zhing mchog tu che ste/ 'di lta ste/ shing rta'i 'phang lo tsam mo/ /pad+ma'i rtsa ba rnams che zhing mchog tu che ste/ 'di lta ste/ skyes bu chen po'i brla tsam mo/ /ro mngar zhing mchog tu mngar te/ 'di lta ste/ sbrang
22a6(mdo 'grel): bu'i sbrang rtsi ma bskol ba bzhin no/ /bcad na yang 'o ma 'dzag go /de'i lam srid du dpag tshad nyi shu dang/ zheng du dpag tshad phyed dang gnyis yod pa/ dbyibs legs shing lta na sdug la/ mdzes pa gser gyi
22a7(mdo 'grel): phye ma brdal cing tsan dan gyis chus chag chag btab pa zhig yod de/ der yang yid du mi 'ong ba/ shing ngam/ gseg ma 'am/ gang ci yang rung ba dag ltung na de mi yin pa rnams kyi rlung gi mthus phyi rol tu 'dor
22b1(mdo 'grel): ro/ /sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi glang po che g.yul ngor chas pa rab tu brtan pa zhes bya ba gzugs bzang zhing lta na sdug la mdzes pa zhig yod de/ me tog ku mu da'i mdog ltar thal dkar du 'dug la/ yan lag bdun shin tu legs
22b2(mdo 'grel): par gnas pa ste/ de'i mgo bo yang dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa ste/ sngo zhing srog chags lham bu chu gsher gyi mdog ltar dbus dmar la mche ba drug yod de/ glang po che rab tu brtan pa'i srid du dpag tshad phyed dang
22b3(mdo 'grel): gsum/ zheng du dpag tshad gcig /'phang du dpag tshad phyed dang gnyis/ mdza' bskor du dpag tshad bdun yod do/ /de'i 'khor glang po che brgyad stong yod do/ /de thams cad kyang gzugs bzang zhing lta na sdug la mdzes pa/ me
22b4(mdo 'grel): tog ku mu da'i mdog ltar thal dkar du 'dug cing yan lag bdun shin tu legs par gnas pa ste/ de dag gi mgo bo yang dbyibs legs shing lta na sdug la mdzes pa ste/ sdo zhing srog chags lham bu chu gsher gyi mdog ltar dbus dmar
22b5(mdo 'grel): la mche ba drug yod pa sha stag ste/ glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa de 'khor dang bcas pa dgun zla ba bzhi ni brag bya skyibs lha ma yin gyi ngos gyi nang na gnas shing 'khod do/ /dpyid zla ba bzhi ni shing sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa'i nang
22b6(mdo 'grel): na gnas shing 'khod do/ /dpyar zla ba bzhi ni rdzing bu dal gyi 'bab kyi nang na gnas shing 'khod do/ /gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa brag bya skyibs lha ma yin gyi ngos kyi nang na gnas shing 'dug pa de'i tshe ni glang po che brgyad
22b7(mdo 'grel): stong po rnams 'di lta ste/ glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa srung ba dang sba ba dang mdzes par bya ba'i phyir brag bya skyibs brgyad stong dag gi nang na nye bar gnas shing 'khod do/ /gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa brag bya
23a1(mdo 'grel): skyibs lha ma yin gyi ngos kyi nang na gnas shing sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa'i nang du 'gro ba na/ res 'ga' ni tha mal pa'i tshul gyis 'gro'o/ /res 'ga' ni 'di lta ste/ lha dang lha'i bu rdzu 'phrul che zhing gang
23a2(mdo 'grel): yang rung ba dang 'dra bar bdag nyid mngon par sprul nas glang po che thams cad kyis nang na dbang che bar grags pa gang yin pa de nyid kyi mgo bo 'am/ rgyab tu zhon te sil snyan dang pheg rdob pa dag rgya cher byed cing 'gro'o/ /gang gi tshe glang po
23a3(mdo 'grel): che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa shing sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa'i nang na gnas shing 'dug pa de'i tshe ni glang po che brgyad stong po 'di dag kyang 'di lta ste/ glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa bsrung ba dang/ sba ba dang/ mdzes par bya ba'i
23a4(mdo 'grel): phyir shing sA la'i phreng ba rim pa bdun po dag gi nang na kha nang du bltas shing 'khod do/ /shing sA la'i phreng ba dang po'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du bltas te 'khod do/ /gnyis pa'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang
23a5(mdo 'grel): kha nang du lta'o/ /gsum pa'i nang du 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o/ /bzhi pa'i nang du 'dug pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o/ /lnga pa'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o/ /drug pa'i nang na 'dug pa gang
23a6(mdo 'grel): yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o/ /bdun pa'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du bltas te 'khod do/ /gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa shing sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa nas rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab par
23a7(mdo 'grel): 'gro ba na/ /res 'ga' ni tha mal pa'i tshul gyis 'gro'o/ /res 'ga' ni 'di lta ste/ lha 'am lha'i bu rdzu 'phrul che zhing mthu che ba gang yang rung ba dang 'dra bar bdag nyid mngon par sprul nas glang po che de dag thams cad kyi nang na dbang che
23b1(mdo 'grel): bar grags pa gang yin pa de nyid kyi mgo 'am/ rgyab tu zhon te bsil snyan dang pheg rdob pa dag rgya cher byed cing 'gro'o/ /gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab kyis nang du zhugs nas rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur
23b2(mdo 'grel): spyod pa de'i tshe glang po che brgyad stong po de dag 'di lta ste/ glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa de bsrung ba dang/ sba ba dang/ mdzes par bya ba'i phyir rdzing bu dal gyi 'bab kyis/ mdza' khor khor yug nas bskor te kha nang du bltas shing 'khod
23b3(mdo 'grel): do/ /gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa rdzing bu ngal gyis 'bab kyi nang nas rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spyad nas phyir byung ba de'i tshe de'i nang na glang po che dbang che bar grags pa gang yin pa de rdzing bu ngal gyis 'bab kyi nang du zhugs
23b4(mdo 'grel): nas pad+ma'i rtsa ba rnams blangs te/ shin tu bkrus shing rab tu gshal nas glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa la 'bul lo/ /gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pas zos shing 'thungs te 'drangs par gyur pa de'i tshe glang po che
23b5(mdo 'grel): gzhan brgyad stong po de dag kyang rdzing bu brgyad stong dag gi nang na rdzing bu re re zhugs nas rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spyod do/ /pad+ma'i rtsa ba dag blangs nas shin tu bkrus shing rab tu bshal te za'o/ /sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams
23b6(mdo 'grel): kyi glang po che'i rgyal po g.yul ngor spyad pa rab tu brtan pa'i mthu ni de tsam mo/ /sems can thams cad ni srungs ma dang bcas shing bsrung ba dang/ skyob pa dang sped pa dang mi 'bral te/ sems can gang dbang chung bar grags shing
23b7(mdo 'grel): bsod nams chung la/ gzi brjid chung ba de dag ni rgya phrag mang po dang/ stong phrag mang po la gcig bsrung ste/ dper na ba lang ngam lug brgya phrag mang po dang stong phrag mang po la gcig srung ba de bzhin du/ sems can gang dbang
24a1(mdo 'grel): chung bar grags shing bsod nams chung la/ gzi brjid chung ba de dag ni brgya phrag mang po dang/ stong phrag mang po la gcig srung ngo/ /sems can gang dbang che bar grags shing bsod nams che la gzi brjid che
24a2(mdo 'grel): ba de dag gi ni brgya phrag mang po dang/ stong phrag mang po dag gis gcig pu bsrung ste/ dper na 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po 'am/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la brgya phrag mang po dang/
24a3(mdo 'grel): stong phrag mang po dag gis gcig pu bsrung ba de bzhin du sems can gang dbang che bar grags shing bsod nams che la gzi brjid che ba de dag la brgya phrag mang po dang/ stong phrag mang po dag gis gcig tu bsrung ngo/ /'dir smras
24a4(mdo 'grel): pa/ ji ste sems can thams cad srung ma dang bcas shing bsrung ba dang/ skyob pa dang/ sped pa dang mi 'bral na ci'i phyir 'tshe ba yod par 'gyur/ smras pa/ srung ma mthu chung zhig yin na de la zil gyis gnon pa las 'tshe ba
24a5(mdo 'grel): yod do/ /srung ma bag med cing bag med par gnas pa zhig yin na ni bag med pa'i rgyu las kyang 'tshe ba rnams yod do/ /srung ma gnyis lhan cig mthun par gyur pas zil gyis mnan nas 'tshe bar byed do/ /mi rnams
24a6(mdo 'grel): chos ma yin pa spyod cing mi rigs pa spyod pa zhig yin na de dag gi chos ma yin pa spyod pa dang/ mi rigs pa spyod pa las kyang 'tshe ba yod do/ /'jig rten bzhag pa/ /bam po gsum pa'o// //sum cu rtsa
24a7(mdo 'grel): gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi mi rnams kyi srungs ma 'di lta ste/ lam po che dang/ srad? dang/ bzhi mdo dang/ sum mdo dang/ dri 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang/ me tog phreng ba 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang/ zong dgram
24b1(mdo 'grel): pa'i gnas rnams dang/ btung ba 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang/ rtag tu myos pa'i gnas rnams dang/ gsod byed kyi gnas rnams su bkod pa dag yod de/ zla ba phyed kyi tshes brgyad la rgyal po chen po bzhi po dag gi g.yog zho shas
24b2(mdo 'grel): 'tsho ba rnams kyi lam po che dang/ srang dang/ bzhi mdo dang/ sum mdo dang/ dri 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang/ me tog gi phreng ba 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang/ zod dgram pa'i gnas rnams dang/ btung ba 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams
24b3(mdo 'grel): dang/ rtag tu myos pa'i gnas rnams dang/ gsong? byed kyi gnas rnams na su zhig 'dug ces 'jig rten 'di thams cad myul te/ ci ste dag gis skyen par tshor na ni de dag gnas mthon po la 'god do/ /ji ste de dag gis skyen par
24b4(mdo 'grel): ma tshor na ni de dag gnas dma' ba la 'god do/ /zla ba phyed kyi tshes bcu bzhi la ni rgyal po chen po bzhi po de dag gi bu rnams kyis lam po che dang/ srang dang/ bzhi mdo dang/ sum mdo dang/ dri 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang/
24b5(mdo 'grel): me tog gi phreng ba 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang/ zong? dgram pa'i gnas rnams dang/ gtung ba 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang/ rtag tu myos pa'i gnas rnams dang/ gsod byed kyi gnas rnams na su zhig 'dug ces 'jig
24b6(mdo 'grel): rten 'di thams cad myul te/ ci ste de dag gis skyen par tshor na ni de dag gnas mthon po la 'god do/ /ci ste de dag gis skyen par ma tshor na ni de dag gnas dma' ba la 'god do/ /zla ba phyed kyi tshes bco lnga la ni rgyal po
24b7(mdo 'grel): chen po bzhi po de dag nyid kyi lam po che dang/ srang dang/ bzhi mdo dang/ sum mdo dang/ dri 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang/ me tog gi phreng ba 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang/ zod dgram pa'i gnas rnams dang/ gtung ba 
25a1(mdo 'grel): 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang/ rtag tu myos pa'i gnas rnams dang/ gsod byed kyi gnas rnams na su zhig 'dug ces 'jig rten 'di thams cad myul te/ ci ste de dag gis skyen par tshor na ni/ de dag gnas
25a2(mdo 'grel): mthon po la 'god do/ /ci ste de dag gis skyen par mtshor na ni de dag dma' ba la 'god do/ /bcom ldan 'das kyis kyang 'di skad du dge slong dag zla ba phyed kyi tshes brgyad la ni rgyal po chen po bzhi po dag gi g.yog zho shas 'tsho
25a3(mdo 'grel): ba rnams ni ci mi dang mi ma yin pa'i 'jig rten na mar 'dzin pa dang/ phar 'dzin pa dang/ dge sbyong du 'dzin pa dang/ bram zer 'dzin pa dang/ rigs kyi nang na rgan rabs la rim gro byed pa dang/ don byed pa dang/ bya ba'i rigs
25a4(mdo 'grel): pa byed pa dang/ bsod nams byed pa dang/ tshe 'di dang/ phyi ma la kha na ma tho ba rnams kyis 'jigs par lta ba dang/ sbyin bdag sbyin zhing bsod nams dag byed pa dang/ gso sbyong la nye bar gnas pa dang/ tshul khrims
25a5(mdo 'grel): yang dag par blangs nas 'dug pa dag mang ngam zhes 'jig rten 'di thams cad du myul lo/ /zla ba phyed kyi tshes bcu bzhi la ni rgyal po chen po bzhi po dag gi bu rnams ci mi dang mi ma yin pa'i 'jig rten na myur 'dzin pa dang/
25a6(mdo 'grel): phar 'dzin pa dang/ dge sbyong du 'dzin pa dang/ bram zer 'dzin pa dang/ rigs kyi nang na rgan rabs la rim gro byed pa dang/ don byed pa dang/ bya ba'i rigs pa byed pa dang/ bsod nams byed pa dang/ tshe 'di dang tshe phyi ma la kha na ma
25a7(mdo 'grel): tho ba rnams kyis 'jigs par lta ba dang/ sbyin pa dag sbyin zhing/ bsod nams dag byed pa dang/ gso sbyong la nye bar gnas pa dang/ tshul khrims yang dag par blangs nas 'dug pa dag mang ngam zhes 'jig rten 'di dag
25b1(mdo 'grel): thams cad myul lo/ /zla ba phyed kyi tshes bco lnga la ni rgyal po chen po bzhi po de dag nyid ci mi dang/ mi ma yin pa'i 'jig rten na mar 'dzin pa dang/ phar 'dzin pa dang/ dge sbyong du 'dzin pa dang/ bram zer 'dzin pa dang/ rigs kyi
25b2(mdo 'grel): nang na rgan rabs la rim gro byed pa dang/ don byed pa dang/ bya ba'i rigs pa byed pa dang/ bsod nams byed pa dang/ che 'di dang tshe phyi ma la kha na ma tho ba rnams kyis 'jigs par lta ba dang/ sbyin pa dag sbyin zhing bsod nams dag
