25b3(mdo 'grel): byed pa dang/ gso sbyong la nye bar gnas pa dang/ tshul khrims yang dag par blangs nas 'dug pa dag mang ngam zhes 'jig rten 'di thams cad myul lo/ /ci ste mi dang mi ma yin pa'i 'jig rten na mar mi 'dzin pa dang/ phar mi 'dzin
25b4(mdo 'grel): pa dang/ dge sbyong du mi 'dzin pa dang/ bram zer mi 'dzin pa dang/ rigs kyi nang na rgan rabs la rim gro mi byed pa dang/ don mi byed pa dang/ bya ba'i rigs pa dag mi byed pa dang/ bsod nams mi byed pa dang/ tshe 'di dang tshe phyi ma la  
25b5(mdo 'grel): kha na ma tho ba rnams kyis 'jigs par mi lta ba dang/ sbyin pa dag mi sbyin zhing bsod nams dag mi byed pa dang/ gso sbyong la nye bar mi gnas pa dang/ tshul khrims yang dag par blangs te/ mi 'dug pa dag mang na ni rgyal po chen po bzhi
25b6(mdo 'grel): po rnams sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams lha'i 'dun sa chos bzangs su 'dus shing 'khod pa'i nang du song nas 'di skad du grogs po dag 'di shes par gyis shig /mi dang mi ma yin pa'i 'jig rten na mar mi 'dzin pa dang/ phar
25b7(mdo 'grel): mi 'dzin pa dang/ dge sbyong du mi 'dzin pa dang/ bram zer mi 'dzin pa dang/ rigs kyi nang na rgan rabs la rim gro mi byed pa dang/ don mi byed pa dang/ bya ba'i rigs pa mi byed pa dang/ bsod nams mi byed pa dang/ tshe 'di
26a1(mdo 'grel): dang tshe phyi ma la kha na ma tho ba rnams kyis 'jigs par mi lta ba dang/ sbyin pa dag sbyin zhing bsod nams dag mi byed pa dang/ gso sbyong la nye bar mi gnas pa dang/ tshul khrims yang dag par blangs te mi 'dug pa
26a2(mdo 'grel): dag mang ngo zhes brnyad do/ /de dag las thos nas sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams yid ma rangs shing mi mgu bar gyur nas yid ma rangs pa nyid kyang phyir zlos par byed de/ kye ma grogs po dag mi dang mi ma yin pa'i 'jig
26a3(mdo 'grel): rten na mar mi 'dzin pa dang/ phar mi 'dzin pa dang/ dge sbyong du mi 'dzin pa dang/ bram zer mi 'dzin pa dang/ rigs kyi nang na rgan rabs la rim gror mi byed pa dang/ don mi byed pa dang/ bya ba'i rigs pa mi byed pa dang/ bsod
26a4(mdo 'grel): nams mi byed pa dang/ tshe 'di dang tshe phyi ma la kha na ma tho ba rnams kyis 'jigs par mi lta ba dang/ sbyin pa dag mi sbyin zhing bsod nams dag mi byed pa dang/ gso sbyong la nye bar mi gnas pa dang/ tshul khrims yang dag par
26a5(mdo 'grel): blangs te/ mi 'dug pa mang ba ni mi rnams kyi chos mdzes pa ma yin no/ /rkyen du bab pa ma yin no/ /legs pa ma yin no/ /dge ba ma yin no/ /de ltar na lha rnams kyi tshogs ni yongs su 'grib par 'gyur la/ lha ma yin
26a6(mdo 'grel): rnams kyi tshogs ni mngon par 'phel bar 'gyur ro zhes zlos so/ /ji ste mi dang mi ma yin pa'i 'jig rten na mar 'dzin pa dang/ phar 'dzin pa dang/ dge sbyong du 'dzin pa dang/ bram zer 'dzin pa dang/ rigs kyi nang na rgan rabs
26a7(mdo 'grel): la rim gro byed pa dang/ don byed pa dang/ bya ba'i rigs pa byed pa dang/ bsod nams byed pa dang/ tshe 'di dang tshe phyi ma dang kha na ma tho ba rnams kyis 'jigs par lta ba dang/ sbyin pa dag sbyin zhing bsod nams dag byed pa dang/
26b1(mdo 'grel): gso sbyong la nye bar gnas pa dang/ tshul khrims yang dag par blangs nas 'dug pa mngan ni rgyal po chen po bzhi po rnams sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams lha'i 'dun sa chos bzang du 'dus shing 'khod pa'i nang du song nas 'di skad du grogs  
26b2(mdo 'grel): po dag 'di shes par gyis shig /mi dang mi ma yin pa'i 'jig rten na mar 'dzin pa dang/ phar 'dzin pa dang/ dge sbyong du 'dzin pa dang/ bram zer 'dzin pa dang/ rigs kyi nang na rgan rabs la rim gro byed pa dang/ don byed pa dang/ bya ba'i
26b3(mdo 'grel): rigs pa byed pa dang/ bsod nams byed pa dang/ tshe 'di dang tshe phyi ma la kha na ma tho ba rnams kyis 'jigs par lta ba dang/ sbyin pa dag sbyin zhing bsod nams dag byed pa dang/ gso sbyong la nye bar gnas pa dang/ tshul khrims
26b4(mdo 'grel): yang dag par blangs nas 'dug pa dag mang ngo zhes bsnyad na ni de dag las thos nas sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams yid rangs shing mgu bar gyur nas yid rangs pa nyid kyang zlos par byed de/ kye ma'o grogs po dag 'di ltar mi dang mi ma
26b5(mdo 'grel): yin pa'i 'jig rten na mar 'dzin pa dang/ phar 'dzin pa dang/ dge sbyong du 'dzin pa dang/ bram zer 'dzin pa dang/ rigs kyi nang nas rgan rabs la rim gro byed pa dang/ don byed pa dang/ bya ba'i rigs pa byed pa dang/ bsod nams
26b6(mdo 'grel): byed pa dang/ tshe 'di dang tshe phyi ma la kha na ma tho rab rnams kyis 'jigs par lta ba dang/ sbyin pa dag sbyin zhing bsod nams dag byed pa dang/ gso sbyong la nye bar gnas pa dang/ tshul khrims yang dag par blangs nas 'dug
26b7(mdo 'grel): pa dag mang ba ni mi rnams kyi chos mdzes so/ /rkyen du bab po/ /legs so/ /dge'o/ /de ltar na lha rnams kyi tshogs ni mngon par 'phel bar 'gyur la/ lha ma yin gyi tshogs ni yongs su 'grib par 'gyur ro zhes
27a1(mdo 'grel): zlos so/ /de nas lha rnams kyi dbang po brgya byin gyis lha'i 'khor rab tu dga' la bde zhing yid bde ba skyes par rigs nas/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ 'di ni zla phyed tshes brgyad dang/ /de bzhin bcu bzhi bco lnga dang/
27a2(mdo 'grel): cho 'phrul gyi ni zla phyed la'ang/ /gso sbyong yan lag brgyad pa la/ /shin tu mnyam bzhag gnas byed 'dir/ /nga ci 'dra bar de bzhin 'gyur/ /dge slong dag lha rnams kyi dbang po brgya byin gang 'di skad du/ 'di ni zla phyed tshes brgyad dang/?
27a3(mdo 'grel): de bzhin bcu bzhi bco lnga dang/ /cho 'phrul gyi ni zla phyed la'ang/ /gso sbyong yan lag brgyad pa la/ /shin tu mnyam gzhag gnas byed 'dir/ /nga ci 'dra bar de bzhin 'gyur/ /zhes tshigs su bcad pa smras pa de ni nyes par smras
27a4(mdo 'grel): pa yin gyi legs par gnas pa ma yin no/ /nyes par bstod pa yin gyi/ /legs par bstod pa ma yin no/ /nyes par brjod pa yin gyi legs par brjod pa ma yin no/ /dge slong dag de ci'i phyir zhe na/ lha'i dbang po brgya byin de
27a5(mdo 'grel): ni 'dod chags dang bcas pa/ zhe sdang dang bcas pa/ gti mug dang bcas pa ste/ skye ba dang/ rga ba dang/ na ba dang/ 'chi ba dang/ mya ngan dang/ smre sngags 'don pa dang/ sdug bsngal ba dang/ yid mi bde ba dang/
27a6(mdo 'grel): 'khug pa rnams las yongs su ma grol zhing sdug bsngal las yongs su ma grol lo zhes nga smra'o/ /de bas na des gang 'di skad du/ 'dir ni zla phyed tshes brgyad dang/ de bzhin bcu bzhi bco lnga dang/ cho 'phrul gyi ni zla phyed
27a7(mdo 'grel): la'ang/ /gso sbyong yan lag brgyad pa dang/ /shin tu mnyam gzhag gnas byed 'dir/ /nga ci 'dra ba de bzhin 'gyur zhes tshigs su bcad pas smras pa 'di nyes par smras pa yin gyis legs par smras pa ma yin no/ /nyes
27b1(mdo 'grel): par stod pa yin gyi legs par bstod pa ma yin no/ /nyes par brjod pa yin gyis legs par brjod pa ma yin no/ /dge slong dag dge slong gang dgra bcom pa yin zhing zag pa zad pa/ bya ba byas pa/ byed pa byas pa/ khur bor
27b2(mdo 'grel): ba/ bdag gis don rjes su thob pa/ srid pa kun tu sbyor ba/ yongs su zad pa/ yang dag pa'i shes pas sems shin tu rnam par grol ba des ni gang 'di skad du/ 'dir ni zla phyed tshes brgyad dang/ /de bzhin bcu bzhi bco
27b3(mdo 'grel): lnga dang/ /cho 'phrul gyi ni zla phyed la'ang/ /gso sbyong yan lag brgyad pa la/ /shin tu mnyam gzhag gnas byed 'dir/ /nga ci 'dra bar de bzhin 'gyur zhes tshigs su bcad pa 'di smras na legs par smras pa yin te nyes par smras
27b4(mdo 'grel): pa ma yin no/ /legs par bstod pa yin te/ nyes par bstod pa ma yin no/ /legs par brjod pa yin te nyes par brjod pa ma yin no/ /dge slong dag de ci'i phyir zhe na/ dge slong de ni 'dod chags dang bral ba/ zhe sdang dang
27b5(mdo 'grel): bral ba/ gti mug dang bral ba ste/ skye ba dang/ rga ba dang/ na ba dang/ 'chi ba dang/ mya ngan dang/ smre sngags 'don pa dang/ sdug bsngal ba dang/ yid mi bde ba rnams las yongs su grol zhing sdug bsngal las yongs
27b6(mdo 'grel): su grol pa'o zhes smra ste/ de bas na des ni gang 'di skad du/ 'dir ni zla phyed tshes brgyad dang/ /de bzhin bcu bzhi bco lnga dang/ /cho 'phrul gyi ni zla phyed la'ang/ /gso sbyong yan lag brgyad pa la/ /shin tu mnyam gzhag
27b7(mdo 'grel): gnas byed 'dir/ /nga ci 'dra bar de bzhin 'gyur zhes tshigs su bcad pa 'di smras na legs par smras pa yin te/ nyes par smras pa ma yin no/ /legs par bstod pa yin te nyes par bstod pa ma yin no/ /legs par
28a1(mdo 'grel): brjod pa yin te nyes par brjod pa ma yin no zhes gsungs so/ /'dzam bu'i gling gi khor khor yug na/ 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po'i lam dpag tshad gcig tu gser gyi bye ma bdal te/ rgya mtsho chen po'i
28a2(mdo 'grel): chus pus mo nub pa tsam du yongs su khyab po/ /gang gi tshe 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po 'jig rten du 'byung ba'i tshe rgya mtsho chen po dpag tshad gnyis kyi bar du chu skam zhing med par 'gyur te/ 'khor los sgyur pa'i rgyal po gang nas
28a3(mdo 'grel): gling du 'gro ba de ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i lam yin no/ /bcom ldan 'das kyis kyang 'di skad du/ dge slong dag sngon byung ba 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po glang po rin po che brtags par 'dod pas nyi ma shar ba'i dus kyi tshe glang po rin po
28a4(mdo 'grel): che la zhon nas sa chen po rgya mtsho la thug pa 'di nyid bskor te/ rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor de nyid du song na/ khye'u sus kyi bya ba byed do/ /dge slong dag gzhan yang 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po'i rta rin po che brtag par 'dod pas nyi ma
28a5(mdo 'grel): shar pa'i dus kyi tshe rta rin po che la zhon nas sa chen po rgya mtsho la thug pa 'di nyid bskor te/ rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor de nyid du song nas khye'u sus kyi bya ba byed do zhes gsungs so/ /bsdus pa'i mdo la/ ri dang skye gnas dag dang
28a6(mdo 'grel): ni/ /nam mkha' lding dang nyo tshong dang/ /grang ba dag ni lnga par byas/ /dus tshigs kyang ni tha ma yin/ /'jig rten bzhag pa las tshigs drug pa'o// //mdo la/ srung ma lha'i grong khyer srang rnams rgyal byed pa/ /chos
28a7(mdo 'grel): bzang rgyu ba'i lam dang 'o bas dang skyed mos tshal/ /sa gzhi dang ni yongs 'du rdo dang glang chen rnams/ /lha ma yin rnams kyi yang de dang 'dra ba yin/ /lha'i grong khyer dang lha ma yin gyi grong khyer gyi bar du sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i
28b1(mdo 'grel): lha rnams kyi srungs ma rnams lnga bkod pa la 'di lta ste/ chu na gnas pa'i klu rnams dang/ lag na gzhong thogs kyi lha rnams dang/ phreng thogs kyi lha rnams dang/ rtag tu myos kyi lha rnams dang/ rgyal po chen po bzhi rnams so/ /
28b2(mdo 'grel): gang gi tshe lha ma yin rnams sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams dang/ lhan cig tu g.yul 'gyed par 'dod par gyur pa de'i tshe/ dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa/ 'di lta ste/ glang po che'i tshogs dang/ rta'i tshogs dang/ shing
28b3(mdo 'grel): rta'i tshogs dang/ dpung bu chung gi tshogs rnams go cha gyon no/ /go cha rnam pa bzhi gyon pa la 'di lta ste/ gser las byas pa dang/ dngul las byas pa dang/ bai DUrya las byas pa dang/ shel las byas pa rnams so/ /
28b4(mdo 'grel): go cha rnam pa bzhi gser las byas pa dang/ dngul las byas pa dang/ bai DUrya las byas pa dang/ shel las byas pa rnams bgos nas/ mtshon cha bzhi la 'di lta ste/ ral gri dang/ mdung dang/ 'phang mdung dang/ gzhu
28b5(mdo 'grel): rnams so/ /mtshon cha rnam pa bzhi ral gri dang/ mdung dang/ 'phang mdung dang/ gzhu rnams blangs nas sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams dang 'gyed pa'i phyir lha ma yin gyi grong khyer nas byung ngo/ /lha ma yin de dag gi
28b6(mdo 'grel): dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa glang po che'i tshogs dang/ rta'i tshogs dang/ shing rta'i tshogs dang/ dpung bu chung gi tshogs rnams kyis go cha bgos te/ go cha rnam pa bzhi gser las byas pa dang/ dngul las byas
28b7(mdo 'grel): pa dang/ bai DUrya las byas pa dang/ shel las byas pa rnams bgos nas/ mtshon cha rnam pa bzhi ral gri dang/ mdung dang/ 'phang mdung dang/ gzhu rnams blangs te/ sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams dang
29a1(mdo 'grel): 'gyed pa'i phyir lha ma yin gyi grong khyer nas byung ba de dag chu na gnas pa'i klu rnams kyis mthong ngo/ /mthong nas chu na gnas pa'i klu rnams kyang dbung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa 'di lta ste/ glang po che'i tshogs
29a2(mdo 'grel): dang/ rta'i tshogs dang/ shing rta'i tshogs dang/ dpung bu chung gi tshogs rnams kyang go cha bgos go cha rnam pa bzhi gser las byas pa dang/ dngul las byas pa dang/ bai DUrya las byas pa dang/ shel las byas pa
29a3(mdo 'grel): rnams bgos nas/ mtshon cha rnam pa bzhi ral gri dang/ mdung dang/ 'phang mdung/ gzhu rnams blangs te/ lha ma yin rnams dang/ lhan cig tu g.yul 'gyed do/ /der ji ste klu rnams rgyal te/ lha ma yin
29a4(mdo 'grel): rnams pham par gyur na ni klu rnams kyis lha ma yin thub cing rdugs par byas te pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par byas nas lha ma yin gyi grong khyer du 'gro bar 'gyur ro/ /ji ste lha ma yin rnams rgyal te/ klu rnams
29a5(mdo 'grel): pham na ni lha ma yin rnams kyis sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi srung ma dang po klu rnams thub cing rdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par byas nas/ rgya mtsho chen po nas ri'i rgyal po ri rab kyi bar
29a6(mdo 'grel): rim dang po gang na lag na gzhong thogs kyi lha rnams 'khod par rjes shing 'gro'o/ /de nas lag na gzhong thogs kyi lha rnams dang/ chu na gnas pa'i klu rnams dang/ srung ma gnyis gcig tu 'dus par gyur nas/ lha
29a7(mdo 'grel): ma yin dang/ lhan cig tu g.yul 'gyed do/ /der ji ste srung ma gnyis rgyal te/ lha ma yin rnams pham na ni srung ma gnyis kyis lha ma yin rnams thub cing rdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs
29b1(mdo 'grel): par byas nas lha ma yin gyi grong khyer du 'gro bar 'gyur ro/ /ji ste lha ma yin rnams rgyal te/ srung ma gnyis pham na ni sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi srung ma gnyis lha ma yin rnams kyis thub cing rdugs par byas te/
29b2(mdo 'grel): pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par byas nas/ ri'i rgyal po ri rab kyi bang rim dang po nas bang rim gnyis pa lag na phreng thogs kyi lha rnams 'khod par rje zhing 'gro'o/ /de nas phreng thogs kyi lha rnams dang/ lag na gzhong
29b3(mdo 'grel): thogs kyi lha rnams dang/ chu na gnas pa'i klu rnams dang/ srung ma gsum po rnams gcig tu 'dus par gyur nas/ lha ma yin rnams dang lhan cig tu g.yul 'gyed do/ /der ji ste srung ma gsum po rnams rgyal te/ lha ma yin rnams
29b4(mdo 'grel): pham na ni srung ma gsums po dag gis lha ma yin rnams thub cing rdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par byas nas lha ma yin gyi grong khyer du 'gro bar 'gyur ro/ /ji ste lha ma yin rnams rgyal te/ srung
29b5(mdo 'grel): ma gsum po rnams pham na ni sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi srung ma gsum po rnams lha ma yin rnams kyis thub cing rdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par byas nas/ ri'i rgyal po ri rab kyi bang
29b6(mdo 'grel): rim gnyis pa nas bang rim gsum pa gang na rtag tu myos pa'i lha rnams 'khod par rjes shing 'gro'o/ /de nas rtag tu myos pa'i lha rnams dang/ phreng thogs kyi lha rnams dang/ lag na gzhong thogs kyi lha rnams dang/ chu na
29b7(mdo 'grel): gnas pa'i klu rnams dang/ srung ma rnams pa bzhi po rnams gcig tu 'dus par gyur nas/ lha ma yin rnams dang lhan cig tu g.yul 'gyed do/ /der ji ste srung ma bzhi po rnams rgyal te/ lha ma yin rnams pham na ni
30a1(mdo 'grel): srung ma bzhi po rnams kyis lha ma yin rnams thub cing rdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgyab kyi phyogs par byas nas lha ma yin gyi grong khyer du 'gro bar 'gyur ro/ /ji ste lha ma yin rnams rgyal
30a2(mdo 'grel): te/ srung ma bzhi po rnams pham na ni sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyis srung ma bzhi po dag lha ma yin rnams kyis thub cing rdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par byas nas/ ri'i rgyal po
30a3(mdo 'grel): ri rab kyi bang rim gsum pa nas bang rim bzhi pa gang na rgyal po chen po bzhi rnams 'khod par rjes shing 'gro'o/ /de nas rgyal po chen po bzhi po rnams dang/ rtag tu myos pa'i lha rnams dang/ phreng thogs kyi lha rnams
30a4(mdo 'grel): dang/ lag na gzhong thogs kyi lha rnams dang/ chu na gnas pa'i klu rnams dang/ srung ma lnga po rnams gcig tu 'dus par gyur nas lha ma yin rnams dang lhan cig tu g.yul 'gyed do/ /der ji ste srung ma lnga po rnams
30a5(mdo 'grel): rgyal te/ lha ma yin rnams pham na ni srung ma lnga po rnams kyis lha ma yin rnams thub cing rdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par byas nas lha ma yin gyi grong khyer du 'gro bar 'gyur ro/ /ji ste
30a6(mdo 'grel): lha ma yin rnams rgyal te/ srung ma lnga po rnams pham na ni sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi srung ma lnga po rnams lha ma yin rnams kyis thub cing rdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par byas
30a7(mdo 'grel): nas/ ri'i rgyal po ri rab kyi bang rim bzhi pa nas steng gi gzhi gang na sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams 'khod par rjes shing 'gro'o/ /de nas rgyal po chen po bzhi rnams kyi dbang po brgya byin gang na ba der song ste phyin nas lha
30b1(mdo 'grel): rnams kyi dbang po brgya byin la 'di skad ces smras so/ /kau shi ka gang bdag cag srung ma lnga po rnams lha ma yin rnams kyis thub cing rdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par byas nas ri'i rgyal po ri rab bang rim gyi
30b2(mdo 'grel): steng gi gzhir rjes te mchis par mkhyen par mdzod cig /kau shi ka de ltar gang gi dus la bab par dgongs shig /de nas lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis rgyal po chen po bzhi rnams kyi ltar mnyan nas sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams
30b3(mdo 'grel): la smras pa/ grogs po dag gang srung ma lnga po rnams lha ma yin rnams kyis thub cing rdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par byas nas ri'i rgyal po ri rab kyi steng gi bzhir rjes te/ yongs pa shes par gyis
30b4(mdo 'grel): shig/ grogs po dag da ltar gang gi dus la bab pa soms shig/ de nas lha rnams kyi dbang po brgya byin gyis glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa la bsams so/ /de nas glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pas lha'i dbang po brgya
30b5(mdo 'grel): byin gyis mtshan ma rtogs nas/ dper na skyes bu stobs dang ldan pa lag pa bskums pa las brkyang ba 'am/ brkyang ba las bskums pa bzhin du glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa 'dzam bu'i gling nas mi snang bar gyur te/ sum cu
30b6(mdo 'grel): rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyis nang du song ngo/ /song nas mgo sum cu rtsa gnyis mngon par sprul te/ mgo re re la mche ba drug drug/ mche ba re re la rdzing bu bdun bdun/ /rdzing bu re re la pad+ma bdun bdun/ pad+ma re re la sdong bu bdun
30b7(mdo 'grel): bdun/ sdong bu re re la lha'i bu mo bdun bdun/ /lha'i bu mo re re la g.yog mo bdun bdun/ /g.yog mo re re la bsil snyan bdun bdun bdun mngon par sprul te/ mgo bo de dag thams cad kyi nang na khyad par du 'phags pa gang yin
31a1(mdo 'grel): pa de la lha'i dbang po brgya byin zhon no/ /de las gzhan pa'i mgo lhag ma rnams la ni nye ba'i dbang po sum cu rtsa gnyis po rnams zhon no/ /de las gzhan pa'i glang po che rnams la ni de la gzhan pa'i sum cu rtsa gsum
31a2(mdo 'grel): pa'i lha rnams zhon no/ /de shin tu mgyogs te/ dper na 'jig pa'i rlung ngam/ 'chags pa'i rlung bzhin te/ de ltar na lha'i bu mo su yang 'di skad du/ 'di ni bdag gis mdun du 'gro'o zhe 'am phyi nas 'ong ngo snyam du sems pa med
31a3(mdo 'grel): de/ de nas glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi grong khyer lho phyogs kyi sgo nas byung ste/ skyed mos tshal rtsub 'gyur tshal du phyin nas/ rdzu 'phrul mngon par 'du byed pa de btang ste/ 'di lta ste lha
31a4(mdo 'grel): 'am/ lha'i bu rdzu 'phrul che zhing mthu che ba gang yang rung ba dang 'dra bar bdag nyid mngon par sbrul te/ sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams dang lhan cig tu lha'i 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga la 'byor cing ldan par 'gyur te/ rtse zhing dga' la
31a5(mdo 'grel): dga' dgur spyod do/ /rang gi las kyi 'bras bu nyams su myong ngo/ /ji tsam du sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams skyed mos tshal rtsub 'gyur tshal du rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spyod pa de tsam du lus kyang rtsub par 'gyur la/ sems kyang
31a6(mdo 'grel): rtsub par 'gyur te/ de dag lus rtsub pa dang/ sems rtsub pa dang/ g.yul 'gyed pa la mngon par mos par gyur nas dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa 'di lta ste/ glang po che'i tshogs dang/ rta'i tshogs dang/ shing rta'i tshogs
31a7(mdo 'grel): dang/ dpung bu chung gi tshogs rnams go cha gyon te/ dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa glang po che'i tshogs dang/ rta'i tshogs dang/ shing rta'i tshogs dang/ dpung bu chung gi tshogs rnams kyi go cha rnam pa bzhi 'di lta ste/ gser
31b1(mdo 'grel): las byas pa dang/ dngul las byas pa dang/ bai DUrya las byas pa dang/ shel las byas pa rnams bgos so/ /go cha rnam pa bzhi gser las byas pa dang/ dngul las byas pa dang/ bai DUrya las byas pa dang/ shel las byas pa rnams
31b2(mdo 'grel): bgos nas/ mtshon cha rnam pa bzhi 'di lta ste/ ral gri dang/ mdung dang/ 'phang mdung dang/ gzhu rnams so/ /mtshon cha rnam pa bzhi la ral gri dang/ mdung dang/ 'phang mdung dang/ gzhu rnams blangs nas lha ma yin rnams
31b3(mdo 'grel): dang lhan cig tu g.yul 'gyed de/ ji ste lha ma yin rnams rgyal te/ lha rnams pham na ni lha ma yin rnams kyis lha rnams thub cing rdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgyab kyi phyogs par byas nas shing rta byang phyogs su lha'i grong
31b4(mdo 'grel): khyer gang na pa der phyir ldog go /'on kyang lha ma yin rnams lha rnams kyi phyi bzhin du snyegs par byed na ni der lha rnams 'di snyam du sems te/ 'di ltar lha ma yin 'di dag bdag cag gi phyi bzhin du snyegs pa las na yang lan
31b5(mdo 'grel): gnyis su g.yul 'gyed par 'dod do snyam du shes nas lha rnams phyir log te/ lha ma yin rnams dang lhan cig tu g.yul 'gyed do/ /ji ste lan gnyis su yang lha ma yin rnams rgyal te/ lha rnams pham na ni lha ma yin rnams
31b6(mdo 'grel): kyis lha rnams thub cing rdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par byas nas shing rta byang phyogs su lha'i grong khyer gang na bar phyir ldog go /'on kyang lha ma yin rnams lha rnams kyi phyi bzhin du snyegs par
31b7(mdo 'grel): byed na ni der lha rnams 'di snyam du sems te/ 'di ltar lha ma yin 'di dag bdag cig gi phyi bzhin du snyogs pa las na yang lan gsum du g.yul 'gyed par 'dod do snyam du shes nas lha rnams phyir log te/ lha ma yin rnams
32a1(mdo 'grel): dang lhan cig tu g.yul 'gyed do/ /ji ste lha ma yin rnams 'ba' zhig rgyal te/ lha rnams pham na ni lha ma yin rnams kyis lha rnams thub cing rdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par
32a2(mdo 'grel): byas nas lha'i grong khyer du 'jug go/ lha'i grong khyer du zhugs nas sgo rnams bcad de/ lha rnams la lha ma yin rnams kyis mi tshugs kyang 'jigs shing skrags pa dang ldan pa'i sems kyis shas cher gnas so/ /'on kyang lha
32a3(mdo 'grel): ma yin rnams kyis der mi rdzi bzhin du lha ma yin rnams kyang 'di ltar lha rnams ni lha'i grong khyer na 'dug kyang 'jigs shing skrag pa dang ldan pa'i sems kyis shas cher gnas mod kyi/ bdag cag gi der mi rdzi'o snyam du shes pa'i
32a4(mdo 'grel): mthong ba 'jug go/ ji ste lha rnams rgyal te/ lha ma yin rnams pham na ni lha rnams kyis lha ma yin rnams thub cing rdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par byas nas shing rta lho phyogs su lha ma yin gyi
32a5(mdo 'grel): grong khyer gang na bar phyir ldog go /'on kyang lha rnams lha ma yin rnams kyi phyi bzhin du snyegs par byed na ni/ de ltar lha ma yin rnams 'di snyam du sems te/ 'di ltar lha 'di dag bdag cag gi phyi bzhin du snyegs pa las na yang
32a6(mdo 'grel): lan gnyis su g.yul 'gyed par 'dod do snyam du shes nas lha ma yin rnams phyir log ste/ lha rnams dang lhan cig g.yul 'gyed do/ /ji ste lan gnyis su yang lha rnams rgyal ste/ lha ma yin rnams pham na ni lha rnams kyis
32a7(mdo 'grel): lha ma yin rnams thub cing sdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par byas nas/ shing rta lho phyogs su lho ma yin gyi grong khyer gang na bar phyir ldog go /'on kyang lha rnams lha ma yin rnams kyi phyi bzhin
32b1(mdo 'grel): du snyegs par byed na ni/ der lha ma yin rnams 'di snyam du sems te/ 'di ltar lha 'di dag bdag cag gi phyi bzhin du snyegs pa las na lan gsum du g.yul 'gyed par 'dod do snyam du shes nas lha ma yin rnams phyir log ste/ lha
32b2(mdo 'grel): rnams dang lhan cig tu g.yul 'gyed do/ /ji ste lan gsum du lha rnams 'ba' zhig rgyal te/ lha ma yin rnams pham na ni lha rnams kyis lha ma yin rnams thub cing rdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par

32b4(mdo 'grel): 'on kyang lha rnams kyis der mi rdzi bzhin du lha rnams kyang 'di ltar lha ma yin rnams ni lha ma yin gyi grong khyer na 'dug kyang/ 'jigs shing skrag pa dang ldan pa'i sems kyis shas cher gnas mod kyi/ bdag cag gis ni der mi
32b5(mdo 'grel): rdzi'o snyam du shes pa'i mthong ba 'jug go /bcom ldan 'das kyis kyang 'di skad du/ dge slong dag sngon byung ba lha dang lha ma yin dag g.yul du zhugs pa lha ma yin rnams rgyal te/ lha rnams pham na ni lha ma yin rnams kyis lha rnams
32b6(mdo 'grel): thub cing rdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par byas nas/ shing rta byang phyogs su lha'i grong khyer gang na bar phyir ldog go /'on kyang lha ma yin rnams lha rnams kyi phyi bzhin du snyegs par byed na ni/ der lha
32b7(mdo 'grel): rnams 'dir ma du sems te/ 'di ltar lha ma yin 'di dag bdag cag gi phyi bzhin du snyegs pa las na yang lan gnyis su g.yul 'gyed par 'dod do snyam du shes nas lha rnams phyir log ste/ lha ma yin rnams dang lhan cig tu
33a1(mdo 'grel): g.yul 'gyed do/ /ji ste lan gnyis su yang lha ma yin rnams rgyal te/ lha rnams pa man ni lha ma yin rnams kyis lha rnams thub cing rdugs par byas te/ phas par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par byas nas/
33a2(mdo 'grel): shing rta byang phyogs su lha'i grong khyer gang na bar phyir ldog go /'on kyang lha ma yin rnams lha rnams kyi phyi bzhin du snyegs par byed na ni der lha rnams 'di snyam du sems te/ 'di ltar lha ma yin 'di dag bdag cag gi phyi bzhin du
33a3(mdo 'grel): snyegs pa las na yang lan gsum du g.yul 'gyod par 'dod do snyam du shes nas lha rnams phyir ldog ste/ lha ma yin rnams dang lhan cig tu g.yul 'gyed do/ /dge slong dag ji ste lha ma yin rnams 'ba' zhig rgyal te/ lha rnams
33a4(mdo 'grel): pham na ni lha ma yin rnams kyis lha rnams thub cing rdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgya gyis phyogs par byas nas/ lha'i grong khyer mchog tu 'jug go /lha'i grong khyer du zhugs nas sgo rnams bcad de/
33a5(mdo 'grel): lha rnams la lha ma yin rnams kyis mi tshungs kyang 'jigs shing skrag pa dang ldan pa'i sems kyis shas cher gnas so/ /'on kyang lha ma yin rnams kyis der mi rdzi bzhin du lha ma yin rnams kyang 'di ltar lha rnams ni lha'i
33a6(mdo 'grel): grong khyer na 'dug kyang 'jigs shing skrag pa dang ldan pa'i sems kyis shas cher gnas mod kyi bdag cag gis ni der mi rdzi'o snyam du shes pa'i mthong ba 'jug go /dge slong dag 'di ltar snga ma 'das pa'i dus na/ lha dang
33a7(mdo 'grel): lha ma yin g.yul du zhugs pa na lha rnams rgyal te/ lha ma yin rnams pham na ni lha rnams kyis lha ma yin rnams thub cing rdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par byas nas/ shing rta lho phyogs su
33b1(mdo 'grel): lha ma yin grong khyer gang na bar phyir ldog go /'on kyang lha rnams lha ma yin rnams kyis phyi bzhin du snyegs par byed na ni der lha ma yin rnams 'di snyam du sems te/ 'di ltar lha 'di dag bdag cag gi phyi bzhin du snyegs pa las na
33b2(mdo 'grel): yang lan gnyis su g.yul 'gyed par 'dod do snyam du shes nas lha ma yin rnams phyir ldog ste/ lha rnams dang lhan cig tu g.yul 'gyed do/ /ji ste lan gnyis su yang lha rnams rgyal te lha ma yin rnams pham na ni lha rnams
33b3(mdo 'grel): kyis thub cing rdugs par byas te pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par byas nas shing rta lho phyogs su lha ma yin gyi grong khyer gang na bar ldog go /'on kyang lha rnams lha ma yin rnams kyi phyi bzhin du snyegs par byed na ni der
33b4(mdo 'grel): lha ma yin rnams 'di snyam du sems te/ 'di ltar lha 'di dag bdag cag gi phyi bzhin du snyegs pa las na yang lan gsum du g.yul 'gyed par 'dod do snyam du shes nas lha ma yin rnams phyir log ste lha rnams dang lhan
33b5(mdo 'grel): cig du g.yul 'gyed do/ /ji ste lan gsum du lha rnams 'ba' zhig rgyal te/ lha ma yin rnams pham na ni lha rnams kyis lha ma yin rnams thub cing rdugs par byas te/ pham par byas shing rgyab kyis phyogs par byas nas
33b6(mdo 'grel): lha ma yin gyi gong khyer du 'jug go /lha ma yin gyi grong khyer du zhugs nas sgo rnams bcad de/ lha ma yin rnams la lha rnams kyis mi tshugs kyang 'jigs shing skrag pa dang ldan pa'i sems kyis shas cher gnas
33b7(mdo 'grel): so/ /'on kyang lha rnams kyis der mi rdzi bzhin du lha rnams kyang 'di lhar lha ma yin rnams ni lha ma yin gyi grong khyer na 'dug kyang 'jigs shing skrag pa dang ldan pa'i sems kyis shes cher gnas mod kyi/ bdag cag gis ni mi rje'o
34a1(mdo 'grel): snyam du shes pa'i mthong ba 'jug go /dge slong dag sngon byung ba 'das pa'i dus na de lta bur gyur to/ /'di skad du/ gang tshe lha dang lha min lhan cig tu/ /gnyi ga 'dus shing g.yul ni 'gyed pa na/ /
34a2(mdo 'grel): shing rta pa ni nyi zla mtshungs med de/ /lha'i shing rta pa'i mchog yin no/ /zhes kyang bya'o/ /ri'i rgyal po ri rab kyi steng gi gzhi na sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi grong khyer lta na sdug ces bya ba chur dpag tshad nyis stong lnga

39a2(mdo 'grel): bzhi ni dbyibs legs shing lha rnams la mdzes par bris shing legs par bris pa/ tshon sna brgya rtsa gcig gis bris te/ 'jam zhing shin tu 'jam pa ni dper na shing bal gyi 'da' ba 'am/ ras bal gyi 'da' bzhin te/
39a3(mdo 'grel): rkang pa bzhag na ni nams zhes byed la/ rkang pa brteg na ni spyar zhes byed la/ me tog man dA ra ba mang pos pus mo nub pa tsam du yongs su khebs te/ rlung gi mthus me tog rnying pa rnams ni mthor/ me tog gsar ba rnams
39a4(mdo 'grel): ni legs par 'grams te/ 'di skad du/ lha rnams bsod nams dbang gi rkyen gyis na/ /shing rta sna tshogs can na rlung chen ldang/ /me tog rnying pa rnams ni 'thor bar byed/ me tog sar ba rnams ni legs par 'grems
39a5(mdo 'grel): zhes kyang bya'o/ /skyed mos tshal shing rta sna tshogs can gyi nad na rdzing bu zhig yod de/ chur dpag tshad lnga bcu/ zheng du yang dpag tshad lnga bcu/ mdza' skor du dpag tshad nyis brgya yod de/ rdzing bu de yang gser las
39a6(mdo 'grel): byas pa dang/ dngul las byas pa dang/ bai DUrya las byas ba dang/ shel las byas pa'i pha gu rnam pa bzhis brtsigs so/ /rdzing bu de'i phyogs bzhin them skas byas pa yod de/ them skad de dag kyang gsar las byas
39a7(mdo 'grel): pa dang/ dngul las byas pa dang/ baiDUrya las byas pa dang/ shel las byas pa'i pha gu rnam pa bzhis brtsigs so/ /rdzing bu de'i lan kan gser las byas pa dang/ dngul las byas pa dang/ baiDUrya las byas pa
39b1(mdo 'grel): dang/ shel las byas ba rnam pa bzhis kun nas skor te/ chu bsil ba dang/ chu sbrang rtsi lta bur gang zhing/ me tog utpa la dang/ pad+ma dang/ ku mu da dang/ pad+ma dkar pos yongs su khebs la/ chu nas skyes pa'i bya chogs skad
39b2(mdo 'grel): snyan cing 'jebs pa dang/ skad yid du 'ong ba dang/ skad mnyen pa dang/ 'dod dgur bsgyur ba'i gzugs can rnams skad snyan pa 'byin to/ /rdzing bu de'i nye 'khor na me tog gi shing dang/ 'bras bu'i shing yod pa rnams legs
39b3(mdo 'grel): par skyes te shing dbyibs legs la yongs su grub pa ste/ me tog phreng bar bkod pa bzhin du gyur pa ni dper na me tog phreng rgyud dam/ me tog phreng rgyud kyi slob ma mkhas pas me tog gi phreng ba tha gu la brgyud pa dang me tog
39b4(mdo 'grel): gi rna rgyan lags par byas pa bzhin te/ thang las skyes pa'i bya sna tshogs skad snyan cing 'jebs pa dang/ skad yid du 'ong ba dang/ skad snyan pa dang/ 'dod dgur bsgyur ba'i gzugs can rnams skad snyan pa 'byin to/ /dpag
39b5(mdo 'grel): bsam gyi shing sngon po dang/ ser po dang/ dmar po dang/ dkar po rnam pa bzhi yod do/ /bzhag gos sngon po dang/ ser po dang/ dmar po dang dkar po rnam pa bzhi yod do/ /dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos sngon
39b6(mdo 'grel): po dang/ ser po dang/ dmar po dang/ dkar po rnam pa bzhi yod do/ /rgyan sna tshogs lag rgyan dang/ rkang rgyan dang/ rgyan snang ba dang/ mi snang ba dag 'byung ba'i shing dag yod do/ /rol mo'i cha byad sna tshogs 'di lta
39b7(mdo 'grel): ste/ pi bang dang/ gling bu dang/ pi bang rgyud gsum pa dang/ 'khar rnga dang/ ham shang rnams 'byung ba'i shing dag yod do/ /lha 'am lha'i bu mo rnams kyis ji lta bur 'dod par sems bskyed ma thag tu de lta bur de dag gi
40a1(mdo 'grel): lag tu 'ong bar 'gyur ro/ /bdud rtsi rnam pa bzhi dang/ sbrang rtsi dang/ sbrang chang gi btung ba dag kyang yod do/ /yang thog rnams dang khang pa brtsigs pa rnams dang/ khyim rnams dang/ khang bzangs rnams dang/
40a2(mdo 'grel): bsil khang rnams dang/ ltad mo lta ba'i sa rnams dang/ zam pa rnams bud med kyi tshogs kyis mdzes par byas shing/ lha'i bu mo mang pos brten pa dang/ sil snyan dang/ pheg rdob pa dag gi sgra snyan pa sgrogs pa dang/
40a3(mdo 'grel): di sna tshogs kyis legs par bsgos pa dang/ kha zas dang btung ba dang ldan pa dag yod de/ de na sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams 'khor dang bcas pa rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spyod de/ rang gi las kyi 'bras bu nyams
40a4(mdo 'grel): su myong ngo/ /de'i lam chur dpag tshad nyi shu/ zheng du dpag tshad phyed dang gnyis pa dbyibs legs shing lta na sdug la mdzes pa gser gyi phye ma bdal cing tsan dan gyi chus chag chag btab pa yod de/ de'i glo g.yas g.yon
40a5(mdo 'grel): na me tog gi shing dang/ 'bras bu'i shing sna tshogs yod pa rnams legs par skyes shing dbyibs legs la yongs su grub pa ste/ me tog phreng bar bkod pa bzhin du gyur pa ni dper na/ me tog phreng rgyud dam/ me tog
40a6(mdo 'grel): phreng rgyud kyi slob ma mkhas pas me tog gi phreng ba tha gul brgyus pa dang/ me tog rna rgyan legs par byas pa bzhin te/ thang las skyes pa'i bya sna tshogs skad snyan cing 'jebs pa dang/ skad yid du 'ong ba dang/ skad snyan pa
40a7(mdo 'grel): dang/ 'dod dgur bsgyur ba'i gzugs can rnams skad snyan pa 'byin to/ /dpag bsam gyi shing sngon po dang/ ser po dang/ dmar po dang/ dkar po rnam pa bzhi yod do/ /bzhag gos sngon po dang/ ser po dang/ dmar po
40b1(mdo 'grel): dang/ dkar po rnam pa bzhi yod do/ /dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos sngon po dang/ ser po dang/ dmar po dang/ dkar po rnam pa bzhi yod do/ /rol mo'i cha byang sna tshogs pi wang dang/ gling bu dang/ pi wang rgyud gsum pa dang/ 'khar rnga
40b2(mdo 'grel): dang/ ham shang rnams 'byung ba'i shing dag yod de/ /rgyan sna tshogs lag rgyan dang/ rkang rgyan dang/ rgyan snang ba dang/ mi snang ba rnams 'byung ba'i shing dag yod do/ /lha 'am lha'i bu mo rnams kyis ji lta bur 'dod par sems bskyed
40b3(mdo 'grel): ma thag tu de lta bur de dag lag tu 'ong bar 'gyur ro/ /lam de na gzhon pa sna tshogs bkod pa 'di lta ste/ glang po che'i bzhon pa dang/ rta'i bzhon pa dang/ shing rta'i bzhon pa dang/ khyogs kyi bzhon pa dag yod de/ lha 'am
40b4(mdo 'grel): lha'i bu mo rnams kyis bzhon pa ji lta bur 'dod par sems bskyed ma thag tu de lta bu'i bzhon pa la zhon par gyur te/ skyed mos tshal shing rta sna tshogs can du dong nas rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spyod de/ rang gi las kyi 'bras
40b5(mdo 'grel): bu nyams su myong ngo/ /ci'i phyir skyed mos tshal gyi ming shing rta sna tshogs can zhes bya zhe na/ smras pa/ skyed mos tshal shing rta sna tshogs can na rdzing bu sna tshogs zhes bya ba dang/ shing sna tshogs dang/ le ma dang me tog dang/
40b6(mdo 'grel): 'bras bu sna tshogs dang/ gos dang rgyan sna tshogs dang/ lnga'i bu mo sna tshogs yod la/ gang gi tshe sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams skyed mos tshal shing rta sna tshogs can na rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spyod da/ de'i tshe
40b7(mdo 'grel): yang rnam pa sna tshogs kyi shin tu rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spyod do/ /rang gi las kyi 'bras bu nyams su myong bas na de'i skyed mod chal gyi ming shing rta sna tshogs can zhes bya'o/ /skyed mos tshal shing rta sna tshogs can gyi shar 
41a1(mdo 'grel): phyogs dpag tshad nyi shu na/ sa gzhi bzang po sna tshogs zhes bya ba zhig yod de/ /chur dpag tshad nyis brgya lnga bcu/ zheng du yang dpag tshad nyis brgya lnga bcu/ mdza' skor du dpag tshad stong yod pa
41a2(mdo 'grel): dbyibs legs shing lta na sdug la mdzes pa/ lan kan gser las byas pa dang/ dngul las byas pa dang/ bai DUrya las byas pa dang/ shel las byas pa rnam pa bzhis kun nas bskor te/ gser gyi lan
41a3(mdo 'grel): kan gyi rten ma dang/ gdang bu gzung gzer ni dngul las byas so/ /dngul gyi ni gser las byas so/ /bai DUrya'i ni shel las so/ /shel gyi rten ma dang/ gdang bu dang/ gzungs gzer ni bai DUrya las
41a4(mdo 'grel): byas so/ /de'i nang gi sa bzhi dbyibs legs shing lta na sdug la mdzes par bris shing legs par bris pa tshon sna brgya rtsa gcig gis bris pa ste/ 'jam zhing shin tu 'jam pa ni dper na shing bal gyi 'da' ba 'am/
41a5(mdo 'grel): ras bal gyi 'da' ba bzhin te/ rkang pa bzhag na ni nems zhes byed/ rkang pa bteg na ni sbar zhes byed la/ me tog man dA ra ba mang pos pus mo nub pa tsam du yongs su khebs te/ de na mi ma yin pa rnams rlung? gi
41a6(mdo 'grel): mthus me tog rnying pa rnams ni 'dor/ me tog gsar pa rnams ni legs par 'grems te/ 'di skad du lha rnams las kyi dbang gi rkyen gyis na/ sa gzhi sna tshogs can rlung chen ldang/ me tog rnying pa rnams ni
41a7(mdo 'grel): 'thor bar byed/ /me tog gsar pa rnams ni legs par 'grems/ zhes kyang bya'o/ /de'i lam srid du dpag tshad nyi shu/ zheng du dpag tshad phyed dang gnyis yod de/ /dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes
41b1(mdo 'grel): ba/ gser gyi bye ma bdal cing tsan dan gyi chus chag chag btab pa zhig yod de/ de'i glo g.yas g.yon na me tog gi shing dang/ 'bras bu'i shing sna tshogs yod pa rnams legs par skyes shing dbyibs legs la yongs su grub ba ste/ me
41b2(mdo 'grel): tog phreng bar bkod pa bzhin du gyur pa ni dper na/ me tog phreng rgyud dam/ me tog phreng rgyud kyi slob ma mkhas pas me tog gyi phreng ba tha gu la brgyus pa dang/ me tog gi rna rgyan legs par byas pa bzhin te/ thang? las skyas pa'i
41b3(mdo 'grel): bya sna tshogs skad snyan cing 'jebs pa dang/ skad snyan yid du 'ong ba dang/ skad mnyen pa dang/ 'dod dgur bsgyur ba'i gzugs can rnams skad snyan par 'byin te/ /dpag bsam gyi shing sngon po dang/ ser po dang/ dmar
41b4(mdo 'grel): po dang/ dkar po rnam pa bzhi yod do/ /bzhag gos sngon po dang/ ser po dang/ dmar po dang/ dkar po rnam pa bzhi yod do/ /dpag bsam gyi shing las byung ba'i gos sngon po dang/ ser po dang/ dmar po dang/ dkar
41b5(mdo 'grel): po rnam pa bzhi yod do/ /rol mo'i cha byad sna tshogs pi bang dang/ gling bu dang/ pi bang rgyud gsum pa dang/ 'khar rnga dang/ ham shang rnams 'byung ba'i shing dag yod do/ /rgyan sna tshogs lag rgyan dang/ rkang rgyan dang/ rgyan snang
41b6(mdo 'grel): ba dang/ mi snang ba rnams 'byung ba'i shing dag yod do/ /lha 'am lha'i bu mo rnams kyis ji lta bur 'dod par sems bskyed ma thag tu de lta bur de dag gi lag tu 'ong bar 'gyur ro/ /lam de na bzhon pa sna tshogs bkod pa 'di lta
41b7(mdo 'grel): ste/ glang po'i gzhon ba dang/ rta'i gzhon pa dang/ shing rta'i gzhon pa dang/ khyogs kyi gzhon pa dag yod de/ lha 'am lha'i bu rnams kyis gzhon pa ji lta bur 'dod par sems bskyed ma thag tu de lta bu'i gzhon pa 'ong bar
42a1(mdo 'grel): 'gyur te/ de la zhon nas sa gzhi sna tshogs can du dor? zhing ci bder gnas par mngon par dga' bar byed do/ /de na lha'i drang srong rnams rang dgar tshangs par spyad pa spyod do/ /de bzhin du lha'i grong khyer gyi
42a2(mdo 'grel): lho phyogs dpag tshad nyi shu na/ skyed mos tshal rtsub 'gyur tshal zhes bya ba zhig yod de/ chur dpag tshad nyis brgya lnga bcu/ zheng du yang dpag tshad nyis brgya lnga bcu/ mdza' skor du dpag tshad stong yod la dbyibs legs
42a3(mdo 'grel): shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa/ gser gyi ra bas kun nas skor te/ ra ba'i 'phang du dpag tshad gcig yod de/ shing rta sna tshogs can ji lta ba bzhin du rgyas par brjod par bya'o/ /khyad par ni 'di yod de/ ci'i phyir skyed mos
42a4(mdo 'grel): tshal gyi ming rtsub 'gyur tshal zhes bya zhe na/ smras pa/ skyed mos tshal rtsub 'gyur tshal na rdzing bu rtsub 'gyur tshal zhes bya ba dang/ shing rnams dang/ lo ma rnams dang/ me tog rnams dang/ 'bras bu rnams dang/ rgyan rnams rtsub
42a5(mdo 'grel): par 'gyur pa dang/ lha'i bu mo rtsub par 'gyur ba rnams yod la/ gang gi tshe sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams skyed mos tshal rtsub 'gyur tshal du rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spyod pa de'i tshe lus kyang rtsub par 'gyur zhing/ sems
42a6(mdo 'grel): kyang rtsub par 'gyur te/ g.yul la mos par 'gyur bas na de'i phyir skyed mos tshal gyi ming rtsub 'gyur tshal zhes bya'o/ /skyed mos tshal rtsub 'gyur tshal gyi dpag tshad nyi shu na/ sa gzhi bzang po rtsub 'gyur zhes bya ba yod de/
42a7(mdo 'grel): chur dpag tshad nyis brgya lnga bcu/ zheng du yang dpag tshad nyis brgya lnga bcu/ mdza' bskor du dpag tshad stong yod de/ sa gzhi bzang po sna tshogs can na ji lta ba bzhin du rgyas par brjod par bya'o/ /lha'i grong khyer gyi nub phyogs
42b1(mdo 'grel): dpag tshad nyi shu na skyed mos tshal 'dres pa'i tshal zhes bya ba zhig yod de/ chur dpag tshad nyis brgya lnga bcu/ zheng du yang dpag tshad nyis brgya lnga bcu/ mdza' bskor du dpag tshad stong yod? la/ gser gyi rabs kun nas bskor
42b2(mdo 'grel): te/ ra ba'i 'phang du yang dpag tshad gcig yod de/ snga? ma rnams na ji skad bshad pa de bzhin du rgyas par brjod par bya'o/ /khyad par ni 'di yod de/ ci'i phyir skyed mos tshal gyi ming 'dres pa'i tshal zhes bya zhe na/ smras pa/ skyed?
42b3(mdo 'grel): mos tshal 'dres pa'i tshal na rdzing bu 'dres pa zhes bya ba dang/ shing rnams dang/ lo ma rnams dang/ me tog rnams dang/ 'bras bu rnams dang/ gos rnams dang/ rgyan rnams 'dres pa dang/ lha'i bu mo rnams 'dres pa yod la/
42b4(mdo 'grel): gang gi tshe sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams skyed mos tshal 'dres pa'i tshal na rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spyod pa de'i tshe yang tshol par 'dres te/ shin tu rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spyod de/ rang gi las kyi 'bras bu nyams su myong
42b5(mdo 'grel): bas na de'i phyir skyed mos tshal gyi ming 'dres pa'i tshal zhes bya'o/ /skyed mos tshal 'dres pa'i tshal gyi nub phyogs dpag tshad nyi shu na sa gzhi bzang po 'dres pa zhes bya ba de/ chur dpag tshad nyis brgya lnga bcu/ zheng du yang
42b6(mdo 'grel): dpag tshad nyis brgya lnga bcu/ mdza' bskor du dpag tshad stong yod de/ sa gzhi bzang po snga ma rnams na ji lta na de bzhin du rgyas par brjod par bya'o/ /lha'i grong khyer gyi byang phyogs dpag tshad nyi shu na/ skyed mos tshal dga' ba'i
42b7(mdo 'grel): tshal zhes bya ba zhig yod de/ chur dpag tshad nyis brgya lnga bcu/ zheng du yang dpag tshad nyis brgya lnga bcu/ mdza' bskor du dpag tshad stong yod la/ gser gyi ra bas kun nas bskor te/ ra ba'i 'phang du dpag tshad gcig
43a1(mdo 'grel): yod de/ snga ma rnams na ji skad bshad pa de bzhin du brjod par bya'o/ /khyad par ni 'di yod de/ ci'i phyir/ skyed mos tshal gyi ming dga' ba'i tshal zhes bya zhe na/ smras pa/ skyed mos tshal dga' ba'i tshal na rdzing
43a2(mdo 'grel): bu dga' ba zhes bya ba dang/ shing rnams dang/ lo ma rnams dang/ me tog rnams dang/ 'bras bu rnams dang/ gos rnams dang/ rgyan rnams dga' ba dang/ lha'i bu mo dga' ba rnams yod la/ gang gi tshe sum cu rtsa gsum
43a3(mdo 'grel): ba'i lha rnams skyed mos tshal dga' ba'i tshal du rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spyod pa de'i tshe yang kun du dga' zhing rab tu dga' la/ dga' zhing yid bde bar gyur nas rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spyod de/ rang gi las kyi 'bras
43a4(mdo 'grel): bu nyams su myong bas na de'i phyir skyed mos tshal gyi ming dga' ba'i tshal zhes bya'o/ /skyed mos tshal dga' ba'i tshal gyi byang phyogs dpag tshad nyi shu na sa gzhi bzang po dga' ba zhes bya ba zhig yod de/ chur dpag tshad
43a5(mdo 'grel): nyis brgya lnga bcu/ zheng du yang dpag tshad nyis brgya lnga bcu/ mdza' bskor du dpag tshad stong yod la/ dbyibs legs shing lta na sdug la mdzes pa te/ sa gzhi bzang po snga ma rnams na ji lta bzhin du rgyas par brjod
43a6(mdo 'grel): par bya'o/ /lha'i grong khyer gyi byang shar gyi mtshams na sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'dus brtol zhes bya ba zhig yod de/ yongs 'dus brtol gyi rtsa ba ni dpag tshad lnga bcu thur du zug go /'phang du ni dpag
43a7(mdo 'grel): tshad brgya yod do/ /yal ga phyir gyes pa ni dpag tshad lnga bcu yod do/ /yongs 'dus brtol gyi yal ga lnga yod de/ yal ga gcig ni shar phyogs dpag tshad lnga bcur 'dud do/ /yal ga gnyis pa ni lho phyogs su
43b1(mdo 'grel): dpag tshad lnga bcur 'dud do/ /yal ga gsum pa ni nub phyogs su dpag tshad lnga bcur 'dud do/ /yal ga bzhi pa ni byang phyogs su dpag tshad lnga bcur 'dud do/ /yal ga steng na ni dpag tshad lnga bcur steng gi nam mkha' khyab par 'dug go /
43b2(mdo 'grel): yongs 'du sa brtol gyi chur dpag tshad brgya lnga bcu yod do/ /zheng du yang dpag tshad brgya lnga bcu yod do/ /mdza' skor du yang dpag tshad sum brgya lnga bcu yod do/ /yongs 'du sa brtol gyi dri rdzi phyogs su ni dpag tshad brgyar
43b3(mdo 'grel): dang ldang ngo/ /rdzi phyogs ma yin par dpag tshad lnga bcur dang ldang ngo/ dpag tshad brgyad cur ni 'od dang kha dog gis lham me lhan ne lhang nger 'dug go /sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol
43b4(mdo 'grel): gyi lo ma ser ba na de'i tshe sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kye ma/ yongs 'du sa brtol 'di lo ma ser ba las nad ni ring bo mi thogs par 'dab ma lhags par 'gyur ro zhes nas kun tu dga' zhing rab tu dga' bas gnas
43b5(mdo 'grel): pa gang yin pa de'i dus kyang yod la/ de'i skabs kyang yod do/ /sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol gyi 'dab ma lhags pa na de'i tshe sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kye ma/ yongs 'du sa
43b6(mdo 'grel): brtol 'di 'dab ma lhags pa las na ring po mi thogs par spal mig 'thon par 'gyur ro zhes nas kun tu dga' zhing rab tu dga' bas gnas pa gang yin pa de'i dus kyang yod la de'i skabs kyang yod do/ /sum cu rtsa gsum
43b7(mdo 'grel): ba'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol sbal mig 'thon pa na de'i tshe sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kye ma yongs 'du sa brtol 'di sbal mig 'thon pa las nad ni ring po mi thogs par sbal mig bye bar 'gyur ro//
44a1(mdo 'grel): zhes kun tu dga' zhing rab tu dga' bas gnas pa gang yin pa de'i dus kyang yod la de'i skabs kyang yod do/ /sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol sbal mig byed pa na de'i tshe sum
44a2(mdo 'grel): cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kye ma yongs 'du sa brtol 'di sbal mig bye ba las nad ring po mi thogs par me tog kha 'bu bar 'gyur ro zhes na kun tu dga' zhing rab tu dga' bas gnas pa gang yin pa de'i dus kyang yod la de'i
44a3(mdo 'grel): skabs kyang yod do/ /sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol gyi me tog kha 'bus na de'i tshe sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kye ma yongs 'du sa brtol 'di me tog kha 'bus pa las nad ni ring po mi thogs
44a4(mdo 'grel): par me tog kha 'bye bar 'gyur ro zhes nas kun tu dga' zhing rab tu dga' bas gnas pa gang yin pa de'i dus kyang yod la de'i skabs kyang yod de/ /sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol gyi me tog 'bye
44a5(mdo 'grel): ba na de'i tshe sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kye ma yongs 'du sa brtol 'di me tog kha 'bye ba las nad ni ring po mi thogs par me tog gi 'dab ma thams cad yongs su rgyas par 'gyur ro zhes nas kun tu dga' zhing rab tu dga' 
44a6(mdo 'grel): bas gnas pa gang yin pa de'i dus kyang yod la de'i skabs kyang yod do/ /sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol gyi me tog 'dab ma thams cad yongs su rgyas pa na yongs 'du sa brtol gyi ma tog 'dab
44a7(mdo 'grel): ma thams cad yongs su rgyas pa'i dri rdzi phyogs su ni dpag tshad brgyar dang ldang ngo/ /rdzi phyogs ma yin par ni dpag tshad lnga bcur dang ldang ngo/ /dpag tshad brgyad bcur ni 'od dang kha dog gis lham me lhan ne lhang nger 'dug go /
44b1(mdo 'grel): bcom ldan 'das kyis kyang 'di skad du/ dge slong dag sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol gyi rtsa ba ni dpag tshad lnga bcur thur du zug go /'bad du ni dpag tshad brgya yod do/ /yal ga dang/ lo ma dang/ yan
44b2(mdo 'grel): lag rnams ni dpag tshad lnga bcur gyes so/ /dge slong dag sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol gyi lo ma ser ba na de'i tshe sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kye ma yongs 'du sa brtol 'di lo ma ser ba las
44b3(mdo 'grel): nad ni ring po mi thogs par 'dab ma lhags par 'gyur ro/ /zhes nas kun tu dga' zhing rab tu dga' bas gnas pa gang yin pa de'i dus kyang yod do/ /dge slong dag sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol gyi 'dab
44b4(mdo 'grel): ma lhags pa na de'i tshe sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams/ kye ma yongs 'du sa brtol 'di 'dab ma lhags pa las nad ni ring po mi thogs par sbal mig 'thon par 'gyur ro zhes nas kun nas ba? dga' ? zhing rab tu dga' bas gnas pa gang yin
44b5(mdo 'grel): pas de'i dus kyang yod do/ /dge slong dag sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol spal mig 'thon ba de'i che sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kye ma yongs 'dus brtol 'di sbal mig 'thon pa las nad ni ring po
44b6(mdo 'grel): mi thogs par sbal mig 'bye bar 'gyur ro zhes nas kun tu dga' zhing rab tu dga' bas gnas pa gang yin pa de'i dus kyang yod do/ /dge slong dag sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol spal mig bye ba na de'i tshe
44b7(mdo 'grel): sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kye ma yongs 'du sa brtol 'di sbal mig bye ba las na da ni ring po mi thogs par me tog kha 'bu bar 'gyur ro zhes nas kun tu dga' zhing rab tu dga' bas gnas pa gang yin pa de'i dus kyang yod do/ 
45a1(mdo 'grel): dge slong dag sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtal gyi me tog kha 'bus pa na de'i tshe sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kye ma yongs 'du sa brtol 'di me tog kha 'bus pa las na da ni ring po mi
45a2(mdo 'grel): thogs par me tog kha 'bye par 'gyur ro/ /zhes nas kun tu dga' zhing rab tu dga' pas gnas pa gang yin pa de'i dus kyang yod do/ /dge slong dag sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol gyi me tog kha bye ba na de'i
45a3(mdo 'grel): tshe sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kye ma yongs 'du sa brtol 'di me tog kha bye ba las na da ni ring po mi thogs par me tog gi 'dab ma thams cad yongs su rgyas par 'gyur ro zhes nas kun tu dga' zhing rab tu dga' bas gnas pa gang
45a4(mdo 'grel): yin pa de'i dus kyang yod do/ /dge slong dag sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol gyi me tog 'dab ma thams cad yongs su rgyas pa na yongs 'du sa brtol gyi me tog thams cad yongs su rgyas pa'i dri rdzi phyogs
45a5(mdo 'grel): su dpag tshad brgyar dang ldang ngo/ /rdzi phyogs ma yin par ni dpag tshad lnga bcur dang ldang ngo/ /dpag tshad brgyad cur ni 'od dang kha dog gis lham me lhan ne lhang nger 'dug go/ /shing yongs 'du sa brtol thams cad yongs su
45a6(mdo 'grel): rgyas pa'i 'og na sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams dbyar zla ba bzhi lha'i 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga la 'byor cing ldan par 'gyur te/ rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spyod de/ /rang gi las kyi 'bras bu nyams su myong ngo/ /dge slong dag
45a7(mdo 'grel): sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol gyi mthu ni de tsam mo zhes gsungs so/ /bar gyi mdo la/ ring por lo ma ser ba dang/ /de nas 'dab lhags spal mig 'thon/ /spal mig byo dang me tog 'bus/ /me
45b1(mdo 'grel): tog kha 'bye thams cad rgyas/ /shing yongs 'du sa brtol gyi drung na sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi ar mo nig ga lta bu'i rdo leb yod de/ chur dpag tshad lnga bcu/ zheng du yang dpag tshad lnga bcu/ mdza' skor du dpag tshad nyis brgya
45b2(mdo 'grel): 'gad du dpag tshad phyed dang drug dang dpag tshad kyi bco brgyad kyi cha gcig yod de/ dbyibs shing blta na sdug la mdzes par bris shing legs par bris pa tshon sna brgya rtsa gcig gis bris te/ 'jam zhing shin tu 'jam pa ni dper na
45b3(mdo 'grel): shing bal gyi 'dab ma 'am/ ras bal gyi 'dab ma bzhin te/ rkang pa bzhag na ni nem zhes byed/ rkang pa bteg na ni spar zhes byed la/ me tog man dA ra ba mang pos pus mo nub pa tsam du yongs su khebs te/ de'i dbus na lha'i
45b4(mdo 'grel): dbang po brgya byin gyi seng ge'i khri bzang po dang/ sum cu rtsa rtsa gsum pa'i lha lhag ma rnams kyi khri bshams pa yod do/ /de na sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams dbyar zla ba bzhi lha'i 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga dag la 'byor cing ldan par

46a1(mdo 'grel): bsam gyi shing sngon po dang/ ser po dang/ dmar po dang/ dkar po rnam pa bzhi yod de/ bzhag gos sngon po dang/ ser po dang/ dmar po dang/ dkar po rnam pa bzhi yod do/ /dpag bsam gyi shing las byung ba'i
46a2(mdo 'grel): gos sngon po dang/ ser po dang/ dmar po dang/ dkar po rnam pa bzhi yod do/ /rol mo'i cha byad sna tshogs 'di lta ste/ pi bang dang/ gling bu dang/ pi bang rgyud gsum pa dang/ 'khar rnga dang/ ham shang rnams 'byung ba'i shing dag
46a3(mdo 'grel): yod do/ /rgyan sna tshogs lag rgyan dang/ rkang rgyan dang/ rgyan sna ba dang/ mi snang ba rnams 'byung ba'i shing dag yod do/ /lha 'am lha'i bu mo rnams kyis ji lta bur 'dod par sems bskyed ma thag tu de lta bur de dag gi lag tu
46a4(mdo 'grel): 'ong bar 'gyur ro/ /bdud rtsi rnam pa bzhi dang/ sbrang rtsi dang sbrang chang gi btung ba dag kyang yod do/ /yang thog rnams dang/ khang ba brtsegs pa rnams dang/ khyim rnams dang/ khang bzang rnams dang/ bsil khang rnams dang/

46a7(mdo 'grel): gi las kyi 'bras bu nyams su myong ngo/ /sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi glang po che'i rgyal po skyed mos tshal du spyad pas srung gi bu zhes bya ba gzugs bzang zhing lta na sdug la mdzes pa zhig yod de/ me tog ku mu da'i mdog
46b1(mdo 'grel): lta bur thal dkar du 'dug la/ yan lag bdun legs par gnas te/ de'i mgo bo dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes te/ sngo zhing srog chags lham bu chu gsher gyi mdog ltar dbus dmar la mche ba drug yod de/ glang po che'i
46b2(mdo 'grel): rgyal po sa srung gi bu'i srid du dpag tshad phyed dang gsum/ zheng du dpag tshad gcig/ 'phang du dpag tshad phyed dang gnyis/ mdza' skor du dpag tshad bdun yod do/ /glang po che'i rgyal po sa srung gi bu'i 'khor glang po che brgyad stong

46b7(mdo 'grel): bo lhag ma rnams la ni nye ba'i dbang po sum cu rtsa gnyis po rnams zhon no/ /glang po che lhag ma rnams la ni sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams zhon no/ /de shin tu mgyogs te dper na 'jig pa'i rlung ngam 'chags pa'i rlung bzhin
47a1(mdo 'grel): te/ de na lha 'am lha'i bu mo su yang 'di ni bdag gi mdun du 'gro'o zhe 'am/ phyi nas 'ong ngo snyam du sems pa med do/ /de nas glang po che'i rgyal po sa srung gi bus sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams so sor grong khyer
47a2(mdo 'grel): gyi sgo nas bston no/ /bton nas so sor skyed mos tshal du phyin par byas te/ rdzu 'phrul mngon par 'du byed pa de btang nas 'di lta ste/ lha 'am lha'i bu rdzu 'phrul che zhing mthu che ba gang yang rung ba dang 'dra bar bdag nyid mngon par sprul nas/
47a3(mdo 'grel): lha'i 'dod pa lnga dag la 'byor cing ldan par gyur te/ /rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spyod do/ /ji ltar brgya byin lha'i dbang po sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi rgyal srid kyi dbang phyug la dbang byed pa de bzhin du/ lha ma yin gyi dbang

47b1(mdo 'grel): kun dga' ra ba rnams yin no/ /sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi sa bzhi bzang po 'di lta ste/ sna tshogs dang/ rtsub 'gyur dang/ 'dres pa dang/ dga' ba ji lta ba de bzhin du/ lha ma yin rnams kyi sa gzhi bzang po bzhi yang kun tu dga' ba ma

49a7(mdo 'grel): bu'i gling du nyi ma phyed du gyur pa de'i tshe shar gyi lus 'phags su ni nyi ma nub po/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan na ni nam phyed do/ /nub kyi ba lang spyod kyi gling na ni nyi ma 'char ro/ /gang gi tshe 'dzam bu'i gling na nyi ma nub pa de'i tshe/ shar gyi lus
49b1(mdo 'grel): 'phags gling na ni nam phyed do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan na ni nyi ma 'char ro/ /nub kyi ba lang spyod kyi gling na ni nyi ma phyed do/ /gang gi tshe 'dzam bu'i gling na nam phyed du gyur pa de'i tshe shar gyi lus 'phags kyi gling na ni nyi ma 'char ro/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan na ni
49b2(mdo 'grel): nyi ma phyed do/ /nub kyi ba lang spyod kyi gling na ni nyi ma nub po/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling thog mar byas te bshad pa de bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags dang/ byang gi sgra mi snyan dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod kyang thog mar byas te thams cad brjod
49b3(mdo 'grel): par bya'o/ /'dzam bu'i gling gi shar phyogs gang yin pa de shar gyi lus 'phags kyi ni lho phyogs so/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi ni nub phyogs so/ /nub kyi ba lang spyod kyi ni byang phyogs so/ /'dzam bu'i gling gi lho phyogs gang yin pa de shar gyi
49b4(mdo 'grel): lus 'phags kyi ni nub phyogs so/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi ni byang phyogs so/ /nub kyi ba lang spyod kyi ni shar phyogs so/ /'dzam bu'i gling gi nub phyogs gang yin pa de shar gyi lus 'phags kyi ni byang phyogs so/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan
49b5(mdo 'grel): gyi ni shar phyogs so/ /nub kyi ba lang spyod kyi ni lho phyogs so/ /'dzam bu'i gling gi ni byang phyogs gang yin pa de shar gyi lus 'phags kyi ni shar phyogs so/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi ni lho phyogs so/ /nub kyi ba lang spyod kyi nub phyogs
49b6(mdo 'grel): te/ ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling thog mar byas te/ bshad pa de bzhin du byang gi sgra mi snyan dang/ nub kyi ba lang spyod dang/ shar gyi lus 'phags kyang thog mar byas te thams cad brjod par bya'o/ /phyogs ni bzhi yod do/ /shar phyogs dang/
49b7(mdo 'grel): lho phyogs dang/ nub phyogs dang/ byang phyogs so/ /shar phyogs la sems can shar phyogs su 'du shes pa dag kyang yod/ sems can lho phyogs su 'du shes pa dag kyang yod do/ /sems can nub phyogs su 'du shes pa dag
50a1(mdo 'grel): kyang yod/ sems can byang phyogs su 'du shes pa dag kyang yod/ lho phyogs la sems can lho phyogs su 'du shes pa dag kyang yod/ /sems can shar phyogs su 'du shes pa dag kyang yod/ sems can nub
50a2(mdo 'grel): phyogs su 'du shes pa dag kyang yod do/ /sems can byang phyogs su 'du shes pa dag kyang yod/ nub phyogs la sems can shar phyogs su 'du shes pa dag kyang yod/ sems can lho phyogs su 'du shes pa dag kyang yod/ sems
50a3(mdo 'grel): can nub phyogs su 'du shes pa dag kyang yod/ sems can byang phyogs su 'du shes pa dag kyang yod do/ /byang phyogs la sems can shar phyogs su 'du shes pa dag kyang yod/ sems can lho phyogs su 'du shes pa dag kyang yod/ sems

54b2(mdo 'grel): dang bdag gnyis su dbyer med cing tha dad pa ma yin te/ bdag gis bdag ni rdzogs pa yin no zhes nas de dag rlung la bkur stir byed/ btsun par byed/ ri mor byed/ mchod par byed do/ /de dag gis bkur stir byas/ btsun par byas/ ri mor byed/ mchod

54b4(mdo 'grel): pa ji lta bu zhe na/ til med pa'i mi la la zhig gis khron pa brko ba'i mi 'ga' zhig la 'di skad du/ kye sdong po me reg ma dang 'dra ba'i mi/ glang mthong dam zhes smras so/ /des smras pa ma mthong ngo/ /til za 'am mi za smras pa mi za'o zhes so/ /de ltar na sa la nam
54b5(mdo 'grel): mkhar 'du shes pa yin no/ ji ltar na nam mkha' la ser 'du shes zhe na/ smras pa/ ji ltar bram ze la la zhig bong bu'i shing rtas song nas bong bu'i shing rta las babs te/ bong bu'i shing rta phur bu la btags nas phur bu nam mkha' la btab ste/ btsugs nas mog la
54b6(mdo 'grel): dkris te/ sal gan rgyal du nyal ba de bzhin du nam mkha' la sar 'du shes pa yin no/ /lo gcig la dus gcig tu mtshan mo ni yud tsam bco brgyad/ nyin ma ni yud tsam bcu gnyis yod do/ /lo gcig la dus gcig tu mtshan mo ni yud tsam bco brgyad/ nyin
54b7(mdo 'grel): mo ni yud tsam bcu gnyis pa de gang zhe na/ dgung zla tha chungs yar gyi do tshes brgyad la mtshan mo ni yud tsam bco brgyad/ nyin mo ni yud tsam bcu gnyis yod do/ /tshes dgu phan chad ni mtshan mo ni 'bri/ nyin mo ni skye ste/ mtshan mo ni thang cig re ris 'bri'o
55a1(mdo 'grel): nyin mo ni thad cig re res skye'o/ /lo gcig la dus gcig tu nyin mo ni yud tsam bco brgyad/ mtshan mo ni yud tsam bcu gnyis pa yod de/ lo gcig la dus gcig tu nyin mo ni yud tsam bco brgyad/ mtshan mo ni yud tsam bcu gnyis pa
55a2(mdo 'grel): de gang zhe na/ smras pa/ ston zla ra ba yar gyi ngo tshes brgyad la nyin mo ni yud tsam bco brgyad/ mtshan mo ni yud tsam bcu gnyis yod do/ /tshes dgu phan chad ni nyin mo 'bri/ mtshan mo ni skye ste/ nyin mo ni thang cig re res 'bri'o/ /mtshan mo ni thang cig re res skye'o/
55a3(mdo 'grel): lo gcig la dus gnyis su mtshan mo yang yud tsam bco lnga/ nyin mo la yang yud tsam bco lnga pa yod de/ lo gcig la dus gnyis su mtshan mo yang yud tsam bco lnga/ nyin mo yang yud tsam pa bco lnga gang zhe na/ smras pa/ dpyid zla tha chungs yar gyi de tshes
55a4(mdo 'grel): brgyad dang ston zla tha chung yar gyi ngo tshes brgyad la mtshan mo yang yud tsam bco lnga/ nyin mo yang yud tsam bco lnga yod do/ /tshes bzhi yod de/ bzhi gang zhe na/ skad cig dang/ de'i skad cig dang/ thang gcig dang/ yud tsam rnams so/ /skad cig pa brgya nyi
55a5(mdo 'grel): shul ni de'i skad cig go /de'i skad cig drug cu la ni thang gcig go /thang gcig sum cu la ni yud tsam cig go /yud tsam sum cu la ni nyin zhag cig go /nyin zhag sum cu'i cha gcig ni yud tsam cig go /yud tsam gyi sum cu cha gcig ni skad gcig go/
55a6(mdo 'grel): thang gcig gi drug cu cha gcig ni de'i skad cig go /de'i skad cig gis brgya nyi shu'i cha gcig gi skad cig go/ skad cig gi tshad ji tsam zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ bud med bal 'khal ba 'brid gis ha cang mi ring ha cang mi thung bar bal bsnyad pa de tsam gyi yun ni skad
55a7(mdo 'grel): cig gyi tshad yin no/ /de lta bu'i skad cig brgya nyi shu la de'i skad cig go /de'i skad cig de lta bu drug cu la thang gcig go /thang gcig de lta bu sum cu la yud tsam gcig go /yud tsam de lta bu sum cu la nyin zhag gcig go /nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba
55b1(mdo 'grel): gcig go /zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig go /'jig rten bzhag pa las tshigs su bcu pa'o// //gleng bzhi ni yul mnyan du yod pa ste/ bcom ldan 'das kyis 'di skad du/ bskal pa ni grangs med pa bzhi ste/ grangs med pa dag gi bskal pa 'jig
55b2(mdo 'grel): go/ grangs med pa dag gis bskal pa zhig bar gnas so/ /grangs med pa dag gis bskal pa chags so/ /grangs med pa dag gis bskal pa chags par gnas so zhes gsungs so/ /bar gyi bskal pa brgyad cu la ni bskal pa chen po gcig ste/ bar gyi bskal
55b3(mdo 'grel): pa nyi shus ni 'jig rten 'jig go /bar gyi bskal pa nyi shus ni 'jig rten zhig par gnas so/ /bar gyi bskal pa nyi shus ni 'jig rten 'chags so/ /bar gyi bskal pa nyi shus ni 'jig rten 'chags par gnas so/ /'jig pa ni rnam pa gsum ste/ mes
55b4(mdo 'grel): 'jig pa dang/ chus 'jig pa dang/ rlung gis 'jig pa'o/ /'jig pa gsum gyis rtse mo ni 'od gsal dang/ dge rgyas dang/ 'bras bu che ba rnams te/ gang gis tshe mes 'jig pa 'byung ba de'i tshe 'od gsal gyi lha rnams la 'jig pa'i rtse mo thug go /
55b5(mdo 'grel): gang gi tshe chus 'byung ba de'i tshe/ dge rgyas kyi lha rnams la 'jig pa'i rtse mo thug go /gang gi tshe rlung gis 'jig pa 'byung ba de'i tshe 'bras bu che ba'i lha rnams 'jig pa'i rtse mo thug go /mes 'jig pa lan bdun zhing chus 'jig pa lan cig /chus 'jig
55b6(mdo 'grel): pa lan bdun zhing rlung gis 'jig pa lan cig 'byung ngo/ /bar gyi bskal pa ni gsum ste/ mtshon gyi bar gyi bskal pa dang/ nad kyi bar gyi bskal pa dang/ mu ge'i bar gyi bskal pa ste/ bskal pa ni mtshon dang nang dang mu ge gsum gyis mthar thug par
55b7(mdo 'grel): 'gyur ro/ /gang gi tshe mtshon gyi bar gyi bskal pa 'od du cha zhing 'byung du nye bar 'gyur ba de'i tshe mi rnams kyi tshe lo bcu thub par gyur te/ tshe lo bcu pa'i mi rnams kyi nang na gang yun ring du 'tsho ba des lo bcu thub ste dper na da ltar gyi mi rnams kyi nang na gang
56a1(mdo 'grel): yun ring du 'tsho zhing ci legs ci bder rim gro byed pa des lo brgya'am/ cung zad lhag par thub pa de bzhin du/ tshe lo bcu pa'i mi rnams kyi nang na gang yun ring du 'tsho ba des lo bcu thub po/ /tshe lo bcu pa'i mi rnams kyi bu gcig pa
56a2(mdo 'grel): sdug cing yid du 'ong ba la mas legs su smon pa na bdag gi bu lo bcu pa'i bar du yun ring du 'tshe bar gyur cig ces legs par smon lam byed de/ dper na da ltar gyi mi rnams kyi bu gcig pa sdug cing yid du 'ong ba la mas legs su smon pa na 'di skad du
56a3(mdo 'grel): bdag gi bu lo brgya'i bar du yun ring du 'tsho bar gyur cig ces legs su smon par byed pa de bzhin du/ tshe lo bcu pa'i mi rnams kyi bu gcig pa sdug cing yid du 'ong ba la mas legs su smon pa na 'di skad du/ bdag gi bu lo bcu pa'i bar du yun ring du 'tsho
56a4(mdo 'grel): bar gyur cig ces legs su smon par byed do/ /tshe lo bcu pa'i mi rnams kyi bu mo bcas nas zla ba lnga lon pa na khyim thab la gtong bar 'gyur te/ dper na da ltar gyi mi rnams kyi bu mo lo bco lnga'am/ bcu drug lon pa na khyim thab la gtong ba de bzhin du/ tshe
56a5(mdo 'grel): lo bcu pa'i mi rnams kyi bu mo btsas nas zla ba lnga lon pa la khyim thab la gtong par 'gyur ro/ /tshe lo bcu pa'i mi rnams kyi gos kyi nang na skra'i la ba mchog tu gyur te/ dper na da ltar gyi mi rnams kyi gos ka shi ka'i ras phra mo 'am/ zar ma'i ras phra mo 'am/
56a6(mdo 'grel): du gu la'i ras phra mo 'am/ ko tam pa'i ras phra mo mchog yin pa de bzhin du/ tshe lo bcu pa'i mi rnams kyi gos kyi nang na skra'i la ba mchog tu 'gyur ro/ /tshe lo bcu pa'i mi rnams kyi kha zas kyi nad na ko Ta ba mchog tu 'gyur te/ dper na da ltar gyi mi rnam
56a7(mdo 'grel): zas kyi nang na 'bras swa lu'i chan nag po'i bag bsal ba tshod ma dang/ /gu ba dang/ bya sna tshogs dang ldan pa/ mchog yin pa de bzhin du/ tshe lo bcu pa'i mi rnams kyi nang na ko Ta pa mchog tu 'gyur ro/ /tshe lo bcu pa'i mi rnams kyi ro rnam pa lnga nub par
56b1(mdo 'grel): 'gyur te/ lnga gang zhe na/ 'o ma yang yod zho yang yod mod kyi mar mi 'byung ngo/ /til yang yod til gyi phye ma yang yod mod kyi til mar mi 'byung ngo/ /sbrang bu yang yod sbrang rtsi yang yod mod kyi sbrang rtsi'i 'byung ngo/ /bu ram shing yang yod khu ba yang yod mod kyi bu
56b2(mdo 'grel): ram du mi 'gyur ro/ /lan tsha ni gtan med par 'gyur ro/ /tshe lo bcu pa'i mi rnams mtshon chas brgyan par 'gyur zhing mtshon chas bzhag par 'gyur te/ dper na da ltar gyi mi rnams kyi rgyan mgul gdub pa ma/ gdu bu rgyan can nam rna cha gdub 'khor rnams sam
56b3(mdo 'grel): dpung rgyan rnams sam/ lag pa'i rgyan rnams sam/ rkang pa'i rgyan rnams sam/ sor gang? bu gyi rgyan rnams sam/ gser dngul gyi phreng ba thogs pa de bzhin du che lo bcu pa'i mi rnams mtshon chas brgyan cing mtshon chas bzhag par 'gyur ro/ /tshe lo bcu ba'i mi
56b4(mdo 'grel): rnams kyi nang na gang mar mi 'dzin pa dang/ phar mi 'dzin pa dang/ dge spyod du mi 'dzin pa dang/ bram zer mi 'dzin pa de dag bkur ba dang/ gces su byas pa dang/ rab tu bsngags par 'gyur te/ dper na da ltar gyi mi rnams kyi nang na gang mar 'dzin pa dang/
56b5(mdo 'grel): phar 'dzin pa dang/ dge spyod du 'dzin pa dang/ bram zer 'dzin pa de dag bkur zhing gces par bya ba dang/ rab tu bsngags pa de bzhin du/ tshe lo bcu pa'i mi rnams kyi nang na gang mar mi 'dzin pa dang/ phar mi 'dzin pa dang/ dge spyod du mi 'dzin pa dang/ bram
56b6(mdo 'grel): zer mi 'dzin pa de dag bkur zhing gces su byas pa dang/ rab tu bsngags par 'gyur ro/ /tshe lo bcu pa'i mi rnams sems can gcig gis gcig mthong na zhe sdang ba'i sems dang/ bsad pa'i sems nye bar gnas par 'gyur te/ dper na da ltar
56b7(mdo 'grel): gyi mi rnams la ri dags kyi rngon pas dgon pa'i ri dags mthong na shas cher zhe sdang ba'i sems dang/ bsad pa'i sems nye bar gnas pa de bzhin du/ tshe lo bcu pa'i mi rnams gcig gis gcig mthong na/ shes cher zhe sdang ba'i sems dang/ bsad pa'i
57a1(mdo 'grel): sems nye bar gnas par 'gyur ro/ /tshe lo bcu pa'i mi rnams kyi gnas rnams su zhag bdun du mtshon 'byung bar 'gyur te/ de dag gis shing ngam/ gseg ma 'am/ gyo mo 'ang rung ste/ gang dang gang la nom pa de dag thams cad mtshon cha bzhin du
57a2(mdo 'grel): rno zhing 'jebs par 'gyur te/ shin tu rno zhing 'jebs pa de dang/ de dag gis gcig la gcig srog dang bral bar byed de/ gnyen 'dun zad pa dang/ longs spyod zad pa dang/ nor zad par 'gyur ro/ /mtshon gyi bar gyi bskal pa de yang zhag bdun kho nar zad
57a3(mdo 'grel): do/ zhag bdun 'das nas mthar thug par brjod par bya'o/ /de'i tshe gang su yang rung ste/ shi ba de dag thams cad lus dang bral nas sems can dmyal ba rnams su skye bar 'gyur ro/ /de na mi gang dag mtshon gyi bskal pa des 'dog cing 'jem par
57a4(mdo 'grel): 'gyur la/ smod cing rnam par smod pa de dag las kha cig ni chu'i rdzong dang/ ri'i rdzong dang/ rdza stug po dang/ nags tshal stug po dag tu zhugs te/ der zhag bdun gyi bar du rtsa ba dang/ chus 'tsho zhing 'dug nas grong dang/ grong rdal dang/ yul 'khor dang
57a5(mdo 'grel): rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor tu phyir log ste/ sems can de dag gcig gis gcig mthong na shas ches byams pa dang/ sdug pa dang/ gus pa dang/ snying brtse ba'i sems nye bar gnas par 'gyur te/ 'di skad du/ kye kye ma sems can gson po
57a6(mdo 'grel): mthong ngo/ /kye kye ma sems can gson po mthong ngo zhes kyang 'dzer to/ /dper na da ltar gyi mi rnams kyi ma la bu gcig pa sdug pa yid du 'ong ba zhig yod la/ zla ba brgyad dam zla ba dgu lon te phrad na shas ches byams pa dang/ sdug pa dang/ gus
57a7(mdo 'grel): pa dang/ snying brtse ba'i sems nye bar gnas pa 'di skad du/ kye ma bu gson po mthong ngo/ /kye ma bu gson po mthong ngo zhes zer? ba de bzhin du/ sems can de dag gcig gis gcig mthong na shas cher byams pa dang/ sdug pa dang/

58a1(mdo 'grel): bar 'gyur to/ /tshe lo lnga bcu pa'i mi rnams 'di snyam du kye ma dge ba'i chos rnams yang dag par blangs pa'i phyir tshe yang nur la kha dog dang stobs dang bde ba dang/ longs spyod dag kyang 'phel bar snang gis/ bdag cag gis yang lhag

58a3(mdo 'grel): cag gis 'dod pa la log par g.yem pa spang bar bya'o zhes nas de dag 'dod pa la log par g.yem pa spong ngo/ /tshe lo lnga bcu pa'i mi 'dod pa la log par g.yem pa spong ba de dag gi bu dang bu mo btsas pa rnams tshe lo brgya thub par gyur to/ /tshe

58a6(mdo 'grel): nas de dag brdzun du smra ba spong ngo/ /tshe lo brgya pa'i mi brdzun du smra ba spong ba de dag gi bu dang bu mo btsas pa rnams tshe lo nyis brgya thub par 'gyur te/ de dag las kha cig ni tshe lo nyis brgya lnga bcu thub par gyur to/ /tshe lo nyis brgya lnga bcu pa'i mi

58b1(mdo 'grel): te 'khod par bya na/ bdag cag gi dge ba'i chos 'ga' zhig yang dag par blangs te 'khod par bya snyam du sems so/ /de dag 'di snyam du kye bdag cag ni phra ma can yin gyis bdag cag gis phra ma spang bar bya'o zhes nas de dag phra ma spong ngo/ /tshe lo nyis brgya lnga

58b4(mdo 'grel): yin gyis bdag cag gis tshig rtsub po spang bar bya'o zhes nas de dag tshig rtsub po spong ngo/ /tshe lo lnga brgya pa'i mi tshig rtsub po spong ba de dag gi bu dang bu mo btsas pa rnams tshe lo stong thub par gyur to/ /tshe lo stong thub pa'i mi rnams 'di snyam du kye dge ba'i chos
58b5(mdo 'grel): rnams yang dag par blangs pa'i phyir tshe yang nur la/ kha dog dang stobs dang bde ba dang/ longs spyod dag kyang 'phel bar snang gis/ bdag cag gis yang lhag par dge ba'i chos 'ga' zhig yang dag par blangs te 'khod par bya na/ bdag cag gis dge ba'i chos
58b6(mdo 'grel): gang zhig yang dag par blangs te/ 'khod par bya snyam du sems so/ /de dag 'di snyam du kye bdag cag ni tshig 'khyal pa can yin gyis bdag cag gis tshig 'khyal pa spang bar bya'o zhes nas de dag tshig 'khyal pa spong ngo/ /tshe lo stong pa'i mi tshig 'khyal pa spong

59a1(mdo 'grel): dog dang stobs dang bde ba dang longs spyod dag kyang 'phel bar snang gis/ bdag cag gis kyang lhag par dge ba'i chos 'ga' zhig yang dag par blangs te 'khod par bya snyam du sems so/ /de dag 'di snyam du kye bdag cag ni brnab
59a2(mdo 'grel): sems can yin gyis bdag cag gis brnab sems spang bar bya'o zhes nas de dag brnab sems spong ngo/ /tshe lo nyis stong lnga brgya pa'i mi brnab sems spong ba de dag gi bu dang bu mo btsas pa rnams tshe lo lnga stong thub par gyur te/ tshe lo lnga stong pa'i mi
